link181: Perezida wa Repubulika y u Rwanda Paul Kagame, yavuze ko imwe mu mpamvu zituma Korea y Epfo ihabwa agaciro gakomeye mu butwererane bw u Rwanda n Afurika muri rusange, ari uko icyo gihugu kizi agaciro k ubusugire n ubwigenge bw ibindi bihugu. Yaboneyeho kugaragaza ko ubutwererane na Korea y Epfo bwatumye u Rwanda ruba igicumbi cyo guhanga udushya ndetse kigera no ku ikoranabuhanga rugezweho mu nzego zitandukanye. Mu nama ihuza Koerea y Epfo n Afurika iteraniye i Seoul kuri uyu wa 4 kugeza ku ya 5 Kamena, Perezida Kagame yahishuriye abitabiriye ko icyo gihugu gikomeje gufasha u Rwanda n Afurika mu kwihuta mu ikoranabuhanga rigezweho. Yagize ati:  Ubufatanye na Korea bwibanze ku guhanga udushya, bufasha kuzana ikoranabuhanga rigezweho mu Rwanda n Afurika mu buryo bwihuse. Iyi nama ibereyeho kutwibutsa ko hari n ibindi byinshi bishobora gukorwa. Uhereye ku ikoranabuhanga ry ubwenge muntu buhangano (AI), ikoranabuhanga rya robo ndetse n irya nikereyeri rizana impinduka zikenewe mu kwimukira ku ngufu zitangiza, ukageza ku bikoresho fatizo by ingenzi, Afurika na Korea bikwiye gukorana bya hafi.  Perezida Kagame yavuze ko Korea itazi agaciro k ubusugire n ubwigenge gusa ahubwo izi n urugamba rukenewe mu kugera kuri Politiki zishingiye ku kubazwa inshingano kandi zidaheza. Nanone kandi ngo ubunararibonye bwa Korea bugaragaza ko igihugu gishobora gutera imbere gihereye ku busa mu gihe cy imyaka 30, ari na ho Perezida Kagame yahereye abaza abitabiriye niba hari igisobanuro  cy impamvu Afurika itaraba umugabane wateye imbere. Ubutwererane n u Rwanda na Korea y Epfo mu guteza imbere ikoranabuhanga butangirana n Ikigo cy ikoranabuhanga mu isakazamakuru  Korean Telecom (KT) Corporation  cyatangiye kugeza mu Rwanda ikoranabuhanga rigezweho mu itumanaho mu myaka isaga 10 ishize. Icyo kigo ni cyo cyatangiye kubaka serivisi z ikoranabuhanga zitandukanye zikoreshwa n inzego za Leta n iz abikorera, kikaba ari na cyo cyagejeje bwa mbere serivisi za internet inyaruka ya 4G mu Gihugu ku bufatanye na Leta. Ubwo bufatanye bwakomeje kwaguka kuko bwavuye ku itumanaho bugera no mu gusangira ubumenyi n ubunararibonye, nyuma y amasezerano u Rwanda na Korea y Epfo byasinyanye muri Kamena 2016 yari agamije kwagura ubufatanye mu nzego z ikoranabuhanga mu isakazamakuru n itumanaho. Korea y Epfo ni yo yafashije mu rugendo rwo gutangiza Ikigo cy Igihugu gishinzwe Ikoranabuhanga mu Itumanaho n Isakazabumenyi (RISA) binyuze mu gusangiza Abanyarwanda ubumenyi, ubuhanga n ubunararibonye mu ikoranabuhanga. Mu kwezi k Ukuboza 2017, ibihugu byombi byasinyanye amasezerano ya miliyari zisaga 5.9 z amafaranga y u Rwanda yifashishijwe mu guteza imbere ikoranabuhanga mu mashuri yo mu Rwanda. Uwo mushinga wagombaga kumara imyaka itatu wibanda ku kubaka ubushobozi bw abarimu basaga 43.000 mu mashuri abanza n ayisumbuye n abashinzwe uburezi mu Turere 446, ku birebana n ikoranabuhanga ryifashishwa mu burezi Mu kwezi k Ukwakira 2022, Guverinoma y u Rwanda n iya Korea byongeye gusinya amasezerano nagamije kwimakaza taransiporo y ibinyabiziga byifashisha amashanyarazi mu kugabanya ibyuka bihumanya ikirere mu Mujyi wa Kigali no mu yindi mijyi. Guverinoma ya Korea ibona u Rwanda nk amarembo yo gukomeza kwagura ibikorwa byayo ku mugabane w Afurika. Afurika ishobora kwihuta mu iterambere Perezida Kagame yaboneyeho kugaragaza ko Afurika ari umugabane ufite ibisabwa byose byawufasha kwihuta mu iterambere, atanga urugero rw umutungo kamere ndetse n abaturage benshi b urubyiruko bafite imbaraga zo gukora byinshi mu gihe gito. Imibare itangwa n Umuryango w Abibumbye igaragaza ko hafi 70% by abagera kluri miliyari 1.4 batuye ku mugabane w Afurika ari urubyiruko ruri munsi y imyaka 30. Perezida Kagame yavuze ko igikenewe ari ubufatanye nk ubwo Afurika ifitanye na Korea bushingiye ku bwubahane, kugira ngo irusheho gutera imbere. Gusa yavuze ko ibyo byose bishoboka hashingiwe ku buryo ibihugu by Afurika bikemura ibibazo by umutekano n ibyimiyoborere, ati:  Urubyiruko rw Afurika rukeneye ayo mahirwe; birashoboka. Afurika ishobora kwihuta cyane mu iterambere kandi nta yindi nzira ihari yaruta kwibanda ku mutekano, ubuzima, uburezi, n ikoranabuhanga.  Yavuze kandi ko Afurika ifite byinshi yishyura mu butwererane n abandi, cyane ko ifite amahirwe y Isoko Rusange ry Afurika (AfCFTA), bityo abaturage b Afurika biganjemo urubyiruko bakaba bafitemo amahirwe yo gutanga umusaruro uhebuje. Yahamije ko Afurika izaba umusemburo w iterambere ry Isi mu gihe Abanyafurika bazareka gukina n ahazaza habo bagakora ibibateza imbere. Ati:  Dukwiye gukomeza inzira y ubufatanye nk uburangwa hagati y Afurika na Korea. Nitubikora dushobora kongera ubutwererane no mu zindi nyungu duhuriyeho mu ruhando mpuzamahanga.  Yasabye Abayobozi b Afurika n aba Korea y Epfo gukorera hamwe no kuzuzanya mu gushyira mu bikorwa imyanzuro y iyi nama igamije kubaka umusingi w ubutwererane buzamara imyaka n imyaka.
link182: Ubuyobozi bwa TikTok bwatangaje ko bwatangiye gukora igerageza rishobora kuzasiga abakoresha uru rubuga nkoranyambaga bashobora gushyiraho amashusho (video) afite isaha imwe. Ni icyemezo ubuyobozi bw uru rubuga nkoranyambaga rwo mu Bushinwa bwatangaje ku wa Kane tariki 16 Gicurasi 2024. Buvuga ko izo mpinduka zigamije gufasha abakoresha TikTok kugira amahitamo menshi ku bwoko bw amashusho bashobora kurushyiraho. Kugeza ubu bamwe mu bakoresha TikTok batangiye guhabwa aya mahirwe yo gushyiraho amashusho afite isaha, bitewe n ibihugu bakomokamo ndetse n ubwoko bwa konti bafite. Gusa kugeza ubu ntiharamenyekana igihe izi mpinduka zizagerera ku bayikoresha bose. Uko imyaka ihita, urubuga rwa TikTok rugenda ruzamura uburebure bw amashusho ashobora kurushyirwaho kuko muri Mutarama hari abahawe uburenganzira bwo gushyiraho afite iminota 30. Ni mu gihe abandi bwemerewe iminota 10 na 20. Igitangira, TikTok yakiraga amashusho atarengeje amasegonda 15. TikTok ni rumwe mu mbuga nkoranyambaga zisigaye zikunzwe cyane ku Isi kuko abayikoresha barenga miliyari 1, ndetse byitezwe ko mu gihe yatangira kwakira amashusho y isaha bishobora gushyira igitutu ku rubuga rwa YouTube na rwo rwemera amashusho afite isaha imwe.
link183: Hashize igihe kirenga umunsi wose internet ibuze mu bice bitandukanye by u Rwanda, aho abanyamahirwe bafite igenda nk akanyamasyo. Ni ikibazo cyakomereye abatari bake cyane cyane abakora ubucuruzi cyangwa batanga serivisi bifashishije murandasi. Ubuyobozi bw Urwego rw Igihugu Ngenzuramikorere (RURA) bwatangaje intandaro y iki kibazo bivugwa ko cyabaye mu bihugu bitandukanye by Afurika y Iburasirazuba n Amajyepfo. Mu butumwa bwacishijwe ku mbuga nkoranyambaga, RURA yagize iti:  Turamenyesha abakoresha internet ko intsinga zinyura mu nyanja zangiritse, bikaba byatumye interinete igira ikibazo. Abakoresha internet bari guhura n ikibazo cyo kugenda buhoro k umuvuduko wayo. Hari gukorwa ibishoboka byose kugira ngo internet ibashe kongera gukora neza.  Iki kibazo bakoresha internet muri Kenya, Tanzania, mu Rwanda no muri Uganda bahereye ku Cyumweru  binubira kuba bakomeje kugorwa no gukore imirimo ikorerwa kuri murandasi. Abatanga serivisi za internet na bo bakomeje gutanga ihumure ko harimo gukorwa ibishoboka byose ngo ikibazo gikemurwe. Iki kibazo cyigeze kuba no mu burengerazuba bw Amajyepfo y Afurika muri Werurwe uyu mwaka. Abakurikirana ikwirakwizwa rya internet bagaragaje ko Tanzania ari yo yaagezweho n ingaruka zikomeye z izo mpinduka aho abakoresha internet bagabanyutse ku kigero cya 30%. Ku mbuga nkoranyambaga nab wo ibigo bitanga serivisi z ihuzanzira rya internet bikomeje gusobanurira abakiliya bakomeje kubihirwa na serivisi zitari nziza bakomeje guhabwa. Airtel Kenya yavuze ko bakomeje gukora kuri iki kibazo ndetse basaba abakiliya kwihangana, ndete na Safaricom yagaragaje ko ikomeje guhangana n icyo kibazo. MTN Rwanda yoherereje abafatabuguzi bayo ubutumwa bubamenyesha ikibazo cyavutse ku ihuzanzira rya internet mpuzamahanga. Ubwo butumwa bwagiraga buti:  Bakiriya bacu, turabamenyesha ko ikibazo cya tekiniki ku muyoboro wa internet muri Afurika y Iburasirazuba kitarakemuka. Turacyari kubikurikirana ngo muhabwe serivisi za internet nk uko bisanzwe. Tubiseguyeho ku mbogamizi byateje.  Uretse ibyo bihugu byo mu Karere bivugwa ko Mozambique, Malawi na Madagascar ari ibihugu byagezweho n iki kibazo nk uko bitangazwa na Cloudfare Radar. Impuguke mu by ikoranabuhanga zemeza ko haba hari umugozi umwe unyura ku nkombe z Afurika y Iburasirazuba mu Nyanja y u Buhinde wacitse ku Cyumweru, mu bilometero 45 uvuye mu Majyaruguru y Icyambu cya Durban  muri Afurika y Epfo. Hari izindi nsinga zihuza Afurika n u Burayi ariko kubera ko ibigo by itumanaho byinshi bivoma ku makusanyirizo y amakuru aba muri Afurika y Epfo birasaba ko imiyoboro ibanza guhuzwa cyangwa se insinga zacitse zigakorwa vuba kugira ngo icyo kibazo gikemuke. Igica izi nsinga ntikiramenyekana ariko bikekwa ko haba hari ababikora kubera urugomo gusa cyangwa se bikaba ari ibibazo bivuka gutyo gusa bikagira ingaruka ku mamiliyoni y abaturage ku mugabane w Afurika.
link184: Ikigo cy Igihugu gishinzwe Ikoranabuhanga mu Itumanaho n Isakazabumenyi (RISA) cyatangaje ko umushinga wo gukora indangamuntu y ikoranabuhanga wongeye gusubukurwa aho izafasha Abanyarwanda kubona ibyangombwa hifashishije sisitemu y Ikoranabuhanga. Umuyobozi Mukuru wa RISA, Bagamba Muhizi Innocent, yabibwiye Abadepite bagize Komisiyo ishinzwe gukurikirana Imikoreshereze y Imari n Umutungo w Igihugu (PAC) ku wa Mbere tariki ya 7 Mata 2024. Yabigaragaje ubwo Minisiteri y Ikaranabuhanga na Inovasiyo ndetse na RISA, batangaga ibisobanuro ku bibazo by imicungire mibi y umutungo w Igihugu, byagaragaye muri raporo y Umugenzuzi Mukuru w Imari ya Leta y umwaka w ingengo y imari warangiye ku ya 30 Kamena 2023. Minisiteri y Ikoranabuhanga no Guhanga Ibishya itangaza ko u Rwanda rwashyize umukono ku masezerano ya miliyoni 40 z amadolari y Amerika (asaga miliyari 51 z amafanga y u Rwanda) yo gushyira mu bikorwa umushinga w indangamuntu korabuhanga. Ubwo yagaragazaga amakosa yakozwe mu micungire y umutungo yagaraye ko muri Raporo y Umugenzuzi Mukuru w Imari ya Leta, Depite Murara Jean Damascene yavuze ko intego ya Minisiteri y Ikoranabuhanga no guhanga Ibishya kwari ugukorera Indangamuntu Koranabuhanga 60% by Abanyarwanda mu 2022/2023 kandi ibi ntabwo byakozwe. Muhizi yavuze  ishyirwa mu bikorwa rya sisitemu y indangamuntu igizwe n umushinga ufite ibyiciro bine. Icya mbere cyerekana ubushakashatsi cyakozwe mbere yo gusinyana amasezerano na Banki y Isi. Icyiciro cya kabiri cyari kijyanye n ubushakashatsi ku kubika amakuru y irangamimerere cyamaze gushyirwamo. Muhizi yavuze ko bagikora ku gushyira amakuru muri sisitemu, aho amakuru arimo gushyirwamo ku buryo yazandikwa neza ku ndangamuntu. Ku cyiciro cya nyuma kizaba kigizwe no gusohora indangamuntu. Yagize ati:  Gahunda yo gutanga amasoko yaratangiye, inyandiko zigaragaza amasoko zishyizwe hanze, kandi abapiganwa batanga ibyifuzo byabo.  Yavuze ko ishyirwa mu bikorwa nyir izina rizatangira nyuma y uko isoko rihawe uritsindiye. Ati:  Mu mezi 18 ari imbere, tuzaba twamaze gukora sisitemu. Turizera ko bizaba birangiye.  Mu 2023, Minisitiri w Ikoranabuhanga na Innovation, Ingabire Paula, yabwiye abagize Inteko Ishingamategeko ko u Rwanda ruteganya ko mu myaka 3 ruzaba rukoresha indangamuntu y ikoranabuhanga. Amakuru asabwa ku ndangamuntu y ikoranabuhanga harimo nomero yayo, izina  rya nyirayo, igitsina, itariki y amavuko, aho yavukiye, ubwenegihugu, n izina ry uwo mwashakanye, nomero ya telefoni, email (niba ihari), aderesi yo guturamo (niba ihari), ifoto ireba imbere, kugaragaza igikumwe cya nyirayo n imboni ya nyirayo. Umunyamabanga Uhoraho muri Minisiteri y Ikoranabuhanga na Inovasiyo, Iradukunda Yves yabwiye Abadepite ko  Indangamuntu y Ikoranabuhanga ari umushinga Guverinoma y u Rwanda irimo gukorana na Banki y Isi, ukaba wagutse uzwatara miliyoni 200 z amadolari ya Amerika wiswe (Rwanda Digital Acceleration Project). Ni umushinga witezweho kuzazamura imibereho y abaturage binyuze mu ikoranabuhanga no guteza imbere gahunda yo guhanga udushya, ukaba waratangiye mu mwaka wa 2022 ukazageza muri 2026. Iradukunda yavuze ko umushinga w imyaka itanu, ushyirwa mu bikorwa na Minisiteri y Ikoranabuhanga no Guhanga Ibishya ku bufatanye n ibigo bitandukanye birimo RISA n Ikigo cy Igihugu gishinzwe Indangamuntu (NIDA).
link185: Ishami rya Polisi rishinzwe ibizamini n impushya zo gutwara ibinyabiziga ryatangiye gukoresha ibizamini bya Perimi hifashishijwe ikoranabuhanga mu kigo cya Busanza giherereye mu Karere ka Kicukiro, Umurenge wa Kanombe, Akagari ka Busanza ku itariki 6 Gicurasi 2024, aho uburyo bwo gukora Demarrage bwahinduye. Hari ibyiza bigaragara muri ubwo buryo bwo gukorera uruhushya rwo gutwara ibinyabiziga nk uko byatangajwe n Umuvugizi wa Polisi, ACP Boniface Rutikanga Yagize ati:  Ikoranabuhanga mu bizamini byo gutwara ibinyabiziga bifite inyungu nyinshi nk umukozi agataha saa kumi n imwe akajya gukora saa kumi n ebyiri agakora ikizamini cye.  Yagize ati:  Ikigo cya Busanza kije kizanye ubusada muri uyu mwuga wo gutwara ibinyabiziga, ubudasa mvuga ni uko kizanye uburyo busukuye, uburyo butavunanye, uburyo butabogamye. Umuntu uzajya gukorera mu Kigo cya Busanza azajya kujya gukorera ikizamini cye ku isaha n igihe yahisemo kimubereye.  Yavuze ko nta muntu uzongera kwirirwa ku zuba, ku muntu uzaba yaje i Busanza, hehe no kwirirwa umuntu anyagirwa ategereje gukora, hehe no guta umunsi wose ku muntu waje gukora ikizamini, uzasaba amasaha yawe uhagere kuri iyo saha. ACP Rutikanga yavuze kandi ko gukora ikizamini bitwara igihe gito kandi ukora ikizamini yicara mu modoka zongera kuvamo asoje. Ati:  Ikizamini cya Busanza, ukuyemo igihe cyo kureba niba koko wariyandikishije wujuje ibisabwa kugira ngo ukore, igice cy icyizamini cyonyine isaha imwe gusa kiba kirangiye. Kuko iyo wicaye mu modoka, ntabwo wongera kuyivamo, uyivamo usoje cyangwa ukayivamo ari uko ugeze mu gice gishobora kuba cyagukuramo ntukomeze, kuko na byo birashoboka hari ikosa wakora mu kizamini bikaba byavamo ko uhagarikwa.  Yongeyeho ati:  Hazaba uburyo bworoshye kandi butabogamye nta gitutu cy umupolisi ngo ntibaseka, babareba nabi nk uko abantu bakunze kubivuga, ntaho uzahurira n umupolisi, uzicaramo wenyine, ni wowe n imodoka n ikoranabuhanga rikubwira icyo gukora. Aho uzahurira n umupolisi ni muri  circulation  naho ntazaba aguha amanota, ni uko iyo umuntu akiri umunyeshuri ataba yemerewe kujya mu muhanda nyabagendwa ari wenyine. Umupolisi bazaba bicaranye ni wa wundi wamufasha igihe agize ikibazo ari mu muhanda nyabagendwa.  Ikoranabuhanga rizanoza umwuga wo gutwara ibinyabiziga Umuvugizi wa Polisi, yavuze ko uburyo bw ikoranabuhanga butaje gukomeza ibintu ahubwo bwaje kunoza umwuga. Ati:  Ntabwo bije gukomeza ahubwo bije kuboneza neza umwuga, kuwutunganya neza ariko abantu bagakora nta kindi gitutu kibazengurutse, iyo bakora kandi bakoresha imodoka nziza zidafite ikibazo nk uko bakunze kujya babinenga.  Ikindi ni ukugira ngo abakora mu mwuga wo gutwara ibinyabiziga baba ari mu rwego rw akazi cyangwa mu rwego rw ikinyabiziga cyabo bwite basobanukirwe neza gutwara imodoka mu buryo butabangamiye abandi, Yakomeje avuga ko kiriya kibuga kizamo ibice byo guca muri  rond point , kikazamo igice cyo kuba wahagarara bitunguranye, kikazamo kuba wahinduranya umuvuduko ku bazaba bakoresha  manuel  bikaba ibice bine haniyongeramo utundi tuntu n ubundi umuntu asanzwe akora ngo agaragaze ko azi gutwara kandi yubahiriza n ibyapa. Yasubije ababyitiranya bakumva ko biriya byiciro bizakomeza no mu bihe biri imbere niba bizahinduka asobanura ko nta kizahinduka kuko ibyiciro byose utwaye akoresheje imodoka ya  manuel  ni nabyo bizanyurwamo umuntu akoresheje imodoka ya  automatic . Yagize ati:  Ni bike bihinduka, abantu bajyaga bakora demarrage iyo bakoresheje imodoka ya  manuel  kuri  automatic  nta demararage izabaho, ikindi kuri  manuel  ha handi tureba uburyo umuntu ahindura umuvuduko, ku ya  automatic  ntibizabaho, ikizabaho igenda ku muvuduko wabugenewe ngo barebe uburyo wubahiriza icyapa kiri mu kibuga.  Ikindi yagarutseho ni uko uzaba afite uruhushya rwo gutwara imodoka ya  manuel  azaba ashobora no gutwara iya  automatic  ati:  Ikindi kizabaho cy ingenzi ni uko uzaba yatsinze gutwara ikinyabiziga akoresheje imodoka ya  manuel  kimwe n utunze uruhushya yatsindiye akoresheje imodoka ya  manuel  bizamushobokera gutwara imodoka ya  automatic  nta kindi kizamini akoze.  yongeyeho ati:  nta nubwo azabazwa kuki yatwaye  automatic . ariko umuntu uzaba yatsindiye imodoka ya  automatic  ntabwo azaba yemerewe gutwara imodoka ya manuel, bizaba bimusaba kuyikorera ikizamini. bivuze ko azaba afite uruhushya rwo gutwara rufitemo inyuguti zigaragaza ko we permis ye imwemerera gutwara n ikinyabiziga cya manuel.  ikigo kizagaragaza ko ubonye permis ayigomba umuvugizi wa polisi, ACP Rutikanga Boniface yavuze ko uburyo bw ikoranabuhanga buzarushaho gufasha kubona uruhushya rwo gutwara ibinyabiziga ku babigomba. yagize ati:  Ntabwo tuje gukomeza permis ahubwo turagira ngo uzayibona azabe ayigomba ni cyo tugendereye. burya iyo uvuga umutekano wo mu muhanda ntucungana cyane n abapolisi kuko kuko uba wishyira mu bibazo, kuko iyo impanuka ibaye ihitana utwaye ikinyabiziga cyangwa yangiza ikinyabiziga cyawe n icy undi wari utwaye, [ ..] umutekano utangira igihe wigaga ikinyabiziga no kugitwara ugahabwa ikizamini, ukagitsinda kandi ubigomba, bihesha gutwara neza, ni byo bihesha umushoferi kuyobora neza ikinyabiziga akurikiza amategeko atabangamiye abandi.  Yavuze ko atari byiza kubaho umushoferi acungana n abapolisi kuko bataboneka ahantu hose ndetse abantu batagomba kumva ko bakorera ikizamini aho bigiye kuko aba atari ho honyine azatwara kuko agomba kwiga imodoka nk uzaba muri Amerika, ukiga imodoka nk uzaba mu kindi gihugu, umuntu ntagomba kwishyiraho imbago mu bitari ngombwa. ACP Rutikanga yasobanuye ko ikigo cya Busanza kije kunganira izindi site zari zihari, ariko ko ari igikorwa kizakomeza kwaguka hirya no hino, kandi ko ibiciro bitahindutse ahubwo ikizahinduka ari igiciro cy imodoka ikoreshwa mu kizamini.
link186: Niba ukoresha imbuga nkoranyambaga za Facebook, Intagram, Threads na Messenger ukaba udashobora kwinjiramo nturi wenyine, kuko uri mu mamiliyoni y abazikoresha badashobora kwinjira muri konti zabo. Ni nyuma y aho kuri uyu wa Kabiri tariki ya 5 Werurwe ku Isi hose hakomeje gukwirakwira amakuru y abantu bagerageza kubikoresha ariko bikanga. Ikibazo kirimo kugaragara ku bakoresha application ndetse n abazikoresha kuri website. Urubuga Down Detector rukurikirana uko imbuga zigenda ziva ku murongo, rwatangaje ko amamiliyoni y abantu kuri ubu batabasha gukoresha imbuga zabo.
link187: Abasirikare n abapolisi b u Rwanda boherejwe mu butumwa bwo kurwanya iterabwoba mu Ntara ya Cabo Delgado muri Mozambique bashyikirije telefoni zigezweho abayobozi b inzego z ibanze. Ni igikorwa cyabaye ku Cyumweru tariki ya 3 Werurwe, aho biteganywa ko izo telefoni zizafasha abo bayobozi mu kurushaho kunoza akazi kabo no gusangiza amakuru ubuyobozi bubakuriye ku byahungabanya umutekano. Abahawe telefone ni abayobozi b Imidugudu 26 bazwi ku izina rya  Wenyekiti , bo mu Karere ka Mo imboa da Praia mu Ntara ya Cabo Delgado, yari yarayogojwe n ibyihebe byo mu mutwe wa Ansar al Sunnah wal Jama a. Ni igikorwa cyitabiriwe n Umuyobozi w Akarere ka Mo imboa da Praia; S rgio Domingos Cipriano, abayobozi batandukanye n abo mu Nzego z umutekano. Kigamije guteza imbere ubufatanye hagati y Inzego z umutekano n abaturage binyuze mu gutanga amakuru ku byahungabanya umutekano n imibereho myiza yabo. Umuyobozi w Akarere ka Mo imboa da Praia, Domingos, yashimiye inzego z umutekano z u Rwanda ku gikorwa cy indashyikirwa bakoze cyo gufasha abayobozi b imidugudu babashyikiriza  telefone zibafasha mukazi kabo ka buri munsi. Yabasabye kuzazikoresha neza bageza amakuru ku gihe, ku nzego zibakuriye n iz umutekano ku bishobora guhungabanya umutekano w abaturage bashinzwe kureberera. Commissioner of Police (CP) Yahya Kamunuga, uyobora umutwe w abapolisi ari na we wazibashyikirije, mu ijambo rye yasobanuriye abahawe telefone; ko ari izo bagenewe hagamijwe kubafasha mu kazi kabo ka buri munsi, cyane cyane mu gusangira amakuru n inzego z umutekano mu rwego rwo kurushaho kubumbatira umutekano n ituze rusange aho batuye mu midugudu. Mo imboa Da praia na Palma ni uduce two mu Ntara ya Cabo Delgado iherereye mu Majyaruguru ya Mozambique, twari twarayogojwe n ibikorwa by imitwe y iterabwoba. Inzego z umutekano z u Rwanda zahageze kuva mu mwaka wa 2021, zifatanyije n inzego z umutekano za Mozambique, kuri ubu zamaze kubihagarika, zitangira ibikorwa byo gusubiza mu byabo abaturage bari barahunze
link188: Abanyamuryango ba Koperative Dukomezubuzima Mudende ikorera mu Murenge wa Shingiro, Akarere ka Musanze bishimiye amahugurwa bahawe agiye kubafgasha gutangira gukoresha mudasobwa bari bamaze umwaka babitse kuva bazigura. Ni Koperative igizwe n abafite ubumuga ihuriwemo n abanyamuryango 20, bavuga ko amahugurwa bahawe n umushinga Feed Future the Rwanda Hanga Akazi, agiye kubafasha kubika inyandiko zabo no koroshya ingendo bakoraga bazijyanira abandi ngo baziboherereze ku ikoranabuhanga. Mukeshimana Clementine, Umunyamabanga wa Koperative Dukomezubuzima Mudende, yabanje gushimira Leta y u Rwanda ikomeza gufasha abafite ubumuga kwisanga mu nzego zose z iterambere ry Igihugu. Yagize ati:  Aya mahugurwa twahawe mu gihe cy ukwezi yatumye twumva ko natwe turi abantu b agaciro, ibi rero bije gukura ho ibira rya hato na hato ry impapuro twajyaga twandikaho, nta nyandiko yacu izongera kubura.  Mukeshimana akomeza avuga ko kubika urutonde rw abanyamuryango na za raporo byajyaga bifata umwanya munini. Na none kandi hari ubwo baburaga uko bigenzura ku birebana n amakuru y umutungo none ubu bigiye kuborohera ndetse ngo bizagabanya ibyago byo kugabanya umutungo. Yagize ati:  Twahawe ikunga y imashini eshatu, izo zose zigomba kujya zibika inyandiko zacu. Bivuze rero ko nta faranga ryacu rizongera kunyerezwa binyuze mu munwa w ikaramu kuko inyandiko zizaba ziri ahantu hanyuranye kandi noneho byakozwe n abanyamuryango uretse bamwe bajya bakoresha abatari abanyamuryango bakora ibyo bishakiye.  Nkurikiyimana Emmanuel we avuga ko batari bazi akamaro n imikorere ya mudasobwa, kandi ngo baterwaga ipfunwe no gukomeza kurebera izo mashini kandi hafi ya bose bazi gusoma no kwandika. Yagize ati:  Tekereza ko tumaranye imashini umwaka ziparitse ariko kubera ko tutari tuzi kuzikoresha zari zigiye kuzagwa umugese none twamenye akamaro kazo.   Kubera imiyoborere myiza natwe abafite ubumuga tugiye kujya twikorera ibyacu mu gihe hari abatubonagamo abantu batagira icyo bamaze. Ikindi ni uko tuzaomeza kwigishanya natwe uburyo bw ikoranabuhanga, kandi tugiye gutangiza gahunda y irembo kuri santeri y ubucuruzi dukoreraho.  Come Ndemezo, Umukozi w umushinga Feed the Future Rwanda Hanga Akazi uterwa inkunga na USAD witwa, avuga ko bafite umushunga wo kwita ku banyamamuryango ba Koperative ariko bibanda ku rubyiruko ndetse n abagore ariko cyane cyane abafite ubumuga. Yagize ati:  Usanga abafite ubumuga bafite ibikorwa binyuranye yemwe n ubushobozi, ariko uburyo bwo kumenyekanisha ndetse no kubyaza umusaruro ibyo bakora, haba ari ukubicunga neza mu buryo bw ikoranabuhanga, usanga baragiye basigara inyuma cyane.  Yavuze ko iyo koperative bayifashije muri byinshi bakomeje kugerageza uburyo bwose bushoboka kugira ngo ibyo bize batangire kubibyaza umusaruro. Akomeza avuga ko uyu mushinga ufite igihe cy imyaka 5, bakaba bizeye ko n izindi koperative zinyuranye zizagerwaho. Arasaba abahuguwe gushyira mungiro amasomo bahawe, bakamenyekanisha ibyo bakora no gukomeza kwigisha bagenzi babo ikoranabuhanga. Yabijeje ko bazakomeza kubakurikirana babafasha no kumenya kwita kuri biriya bikoresho by ikoranabuhanga. Kayiranga Theobald, Umuyobozi wungirije w Akarere ka Musanze ushinzwe imibereho myiza y abaturage, avuga ko  amahugurwa nk ariya  ari muri gahunda ya Leta  aho buri wese agomba kugendana n ikoranabuhanga. Yemeje ko umuntu agomba kubika ibintu bye nk inyandiko binyuze mu ikoranabuhanga, agasaba abo bose bahuguwe kubyaza umusaruro ubumenyi bahawe no kubusakaza ku bandi. Yagize ati:  Ibyo bize babigeze ku bandi babike neza inyandiko zabo, kandi ibyo bakoraga barusheho kubiteza imbere ndetse babibyaze umusaruro kandi abafite ubumuga na bo bumve bashoboye.  Yasabye ababyeyi bababyaye cyangwa barera abana bavukanye ubumuga kutabahisha mu gikari kuko hanze hari amahirwe menshi abategereje kandi na bon go barashoboye. Ati:  Byagaragaye ko ufite ubumuga na we iyo ahawe uburenganzira bwe akigishwa umwuga atanga umusaruro . Koperative Dukomezubuzima kugeza ubu ifite abanyamuryango bagera kuri 300, bakaba bakora ubuhinzi bw ibirayi, kuri ubu bakaba bafite umutungo ukabakaba muri miliyoni 40 harimo inyubako amasambu n inzu.
link189: Ikigo cy u Rwanda gishinzwe isanzure (RSA) n icyo muri Polonye POLSA, kuri uyu wa Kabiri tariki ya 27 Gashyantare 2024, byasinyanye amasezerano agamije guteza imbere uruhererekane rw ikoranabuhanga mu isanzure. Aya masezerano y imikoranire yasinywe mu rwego rwo guteza imbere imikoranire hagati y ibihugu byombi hagamijwe guteza imbere ibikorerwa mu isanzure. Col. Francis Ngabo, Umuyobozi Mukuru wa RSA, yavuze ko u Rwanda rukomeje gusigasira ikoranabuhanga no kuryongerera ubushobozi mu kuzamura iterambere ry uru rwego mu gihugu imbere. Yagize ati :  Gukorana na Polonye binyuze mu kigo POLSA biradufungirira amarembo yo guhanga ibishya ndetse no gusangira ubumenyi mu kuzamura urwego rw iterambere mu by isanzure . Grzegorz Wrochna, Umuyobozi Mukuru wa POLSA, yashimangiye ko imikoranire ya Polonye n u Rwanda azahangana n imbogamizi bahuraga na zo ndetse no guhanga ibishya. Yagize ati:  Imbaraga ziri muri ubu bufatanye, tugamije kuzamura ikoranabuhanga mu isanzure ndetse no gutanga umusanzu mu guteza imbere imibereho myiza y abaturage bacu . U Rwanda na Polonye bibanye neza mu bijyanye na Dipolomasi, aho mu ntangiriro z uku kwezi kwa Gashyantare Perezida wa Polonye Andrzej Duda yasuye u Rwanda. Muri urwo ruzinduko, wabaye umwanya wo kungurana ibitekerezo hagati y abacuruzi ba Polonye n ab u Rwanda ku ishoramari hagati b ibihugu byombi. Icyo gihe kandi u Rwanda na Polonye basinyanye amasezerano y imikoranire mu bucuruzi, mu rwego rw ubumenyi bw Isi, ikoranabuhanga mu kubungabunga ibidukikije n ibindi. By umwihariko mu bijyanye n uruhererekane mu by isanzure hatangijwe imikoranire hagati y u Rwanda na Polonye binyuze mu kigo cy u Rwanda cya Locus Dynamics (LD) na Kompanyi ya Polonye yita ku bijyanye n isanzure SatRev, binjiye mu bufatanye mu iterambere ry Isi mu bugenzuzi bw Ibikorwa remezo by Ibyogajuru. Ni ubufatanye bwitezweho gufasha u Rwanda mu iterambere ry ubumenyi bw isanzure bukazagera no ku bindi bihugu. U Rwanda ni igihugu gishyize imbere guteza imbere uruherekane mu by isanzure bishingiye ku mikoranire n ibindi bihugu ndetse n ibigo bikomeye biri muri uru rwego, mu guteza imbere ubushobozi bw ibikorerwa mu isanzure, amakuru y ibiberayo, ishusho yaho ndetse n imikoreshereze y ibyogajuru. Imibare igaragaza ko Leta z Ibihugu by Afurika zitanga miliyoni nyinshi z Amadolari y Amerika mu gukodesha ibyogajuru no mu gukoresha amakuru yabyo muri za Kompanyi z Ubucuruzi. Ni icyuho RSA yiyemeje kuziba binyuze mu korohereza abacuruzi bifuza gukoresha inzira z isanzure, ku buryo u Rwanda ruzaba irembo ry ibikorerwa mu isanzure ku mugabane w Afurika.
link190: Abantu 70% by abakoresha konti za Mobile Money (MoMo) zisaga miliyoni 16.5 zibarurwa mu Rwanda bavugwaho kuba bishyura ibicuruzwa na serivisi batarinze gutwara amafaranga mu ntoki. Iyo mibare ishimangirwa na Minisiteri y Ikoranabuhanga na Inovasiyo (MINICT) nk umusaruro w ubukangurambaga bwo gushikariza abaturage kwishyurana hakoreshejwe ikoranabunga bwiswe (Twagiye Kashiresi) bwatangijwe na Guverinoma y u Rwanda muri Gicurasi 2022. Iyo Minisiteti yashimangiye ko abahererekanya amafaranga bakoresheje telefoni bageze kuri 70% bavuye kuri 49% mu myaka itatu ishize. Byatangajwe kuri uyu wa Kabiri tariki ya 8 Gashyantare 2024, mu biganiro nyunguranabitekero byahuje Minisiteri y Ikoranabuhanga no Inovasiyo n ibigo by imari baganira ku kunoza uburyo bwo kwishyurana hakoreshejwe ikoranabuhanga mu bigo by imari no mu zindi nzego. Minisitiri wa MINICT Ingabire Paula, yagaragaje ko n ubwo hakirimo imbogamizi mu kwishyurana hakoreshwe ikoranabuhanga, abantu bagenda babyitabira ku buryo bushimishije. Yagize ati:  Urebye mu myaka itatu ishize n uyu munsi uko bihagaze,mfashe nk imibare ya Mobile Money, twavuye kuri 49% ubu tugerengeje ijanisha rya 70%. Bivuze ko hari abantu benshi barushaho kwifashisha uburyo bwo gukoresha telefoni n ikoranabunga muri uru rugendo rwa Kashiresi,ari na yo mpamvu twatangiye ubukangurambaga.  Minisitiri Ingabire yagavuze ko mu bukanguramba bakora ari ho babona imbogamizi zihari bakazikemura aho avuga ko ahakiri ikibazo cy ibikorwaremezo mu itumanaho bigenda byongerwa. Ati:  Tugenda twongera iminara mu gihugu kugira ngo tuzibe cya cyuho  cya za serivisi z itumanaho zitahagera.  Mu mbogamizi MINICT ikagaragaza zikibangamiye gahunda ya yo guhererekanya amafaranga hata harimo kuba ikiguzi kuri serivisi kikiri hejura kuri bamwe na bamwe, ubumenyi buke mu ikoranabuhanga n ibindi. Mu kwimakaza iyi gahunda yo guhererekanya amafaranga mu buryo bw ikoranabuhanga, MINICT yatangaje ko harimo gutegurwa amahugurwa ku bakoresha izi servisi, ndetse no gushaka uko ikiguzi cy abazifashisha cyagabanyuka. Minisitiri Paula yavuze ko ibigo by imari birimo za Banki n ibindi bigo by itumanaho bigomba kunoza imikoranire mu by ikoranabuhanga bagahanahana amakuru ahagije, mu rwego rwo kugabanyiriza ikiguzi cy ukenera ikoranabuhanga mu kwishyura serivisi muri ibyo bigo. Umuyobozi Mukuru wungirije wa Banki Nkuru y u Rwanda (BNR) Soraya Hakuziyaremye, yagaragaje ko ubukangurambaga bwa Twagiye Kashiresi bwabagaragarije imbogamizi zitandukanye. Ati:  Harimo kuba ikiguzi cyo kwishyurana kikiri hajeru, kuba abantu badasobanukirwa n ikoranabuhanga aho usanga hari n abacuruzi badakunda gukoresha  Code  n iyo bazifite . Yakomeje agira ati:  Hari amabanki n abakoresha servisi za Mobile Money bavuga ko serivisi bakora ziba zihenze, turaganira kugira ngo turebe ukuntu byagabanyuka no gukangirira abantu kumva ko kwishyura kuri Kode za Mobile Money ari ubuntu iyo wishyuye ari munsi y ibihumbi bine (4000) bitewe na kompanyi.  Mu bukangurambaga bwiswe  Twagiye Kashiresi  bwatangiye muri Gicurasi 2022, bwageze ku baturage ibihumbi 24 mu Turere 12 tw u Rwanda. BRN irimo gutegura kwagura ubu bukangurambaga bwo kwimakagaza gukoresha ikoranabuhanga mu kwishyurana bugakorwa mu nzego zitandukanye zaba iz ubuhinzi, ubucuruzi buciriritse, uburezi ndetse n ubuzima kandi bukagera  no mu tundi Turere dusigaye tw igihugu.
link191: Minisiteri y Ibidukikije yatangaje ko yakodesheje ubutaka bwa Leta, isosiyete y itumanaho izobereye mu kohereza umuyoboro wa fibre optique no gukwirakwiza ihuzanzira mu itumanaho (TRES Infrastructure Ltd), mu rwego rwo kongera imiyoboro y itumanaho mu gihugu hose. Ni itizwa ry ubutaka bwa Leta, ryari mu myanzuro y inama y Abaminisitiri yashyizwe ahagaragara tariki ya 25 Mutarama 2024. Iyo Kompanyi izakoresha ubutaka bwa Leta bwagenewe kwagura imiyoboro mu gihugu hose. Dr Mujawamariya Jeanne d Arc, Minisitiri w Ibidukikije yatangarije The New Times ko ibibanza byagenewe kwagurirwamo imiyoboro, biherereye mu Turere twa Kamonyi, Nyanza, Muhanga, Ruhango, Nyamagabe, Musanze, Gakenke, Karongi, na Nyagatare. Ati:  Kwagura imiyoboro y itumanaho ni gahunda ya Guverinoma yiyemeje yo gutanga serivisi z itumanaho zizewe kandi zujuje ubuziranenge ku baturage mu gihugu hose.  Yavuze ko ishyirwaho ry iminara muri utwo turere dutandukanye, rigamije kuziba icyuho cyari mu itumanaho no kugira uruhare mu iterambere rusange ry igihugu. Ni icyemezo cyafashwe nyuma y aho hari abaturage bakunze kwinubira kubura ihuzanzira mu itumanaho, mu bice bimwe na bimwe by igihugu. Umwe mu baturage bo mu Karere ka Rubavu, Neza Rodriguez yagize:  Mu Karere ka Rubavu by umwihariko mu Murenge wa Nyakiriba, tuhafite ikibazo cy ihuzanzira mu itumanaho. Tugorwa no kubona interineti.  Imanashimwe Peter, umuturage wo mu Murenge wa Jabana mu Karere ka Gasabo mu Mujyi wa Kigali yagize ati:  Tumaze imyaka 3 tudafite ihuzanzira mu itumanaho muri Bweramvura mu Murenge wa Jabana. Guhamagara, kohereza ubutumwa bugufi cyangwa gukoresha interineti ntabwo bigenda neza. Kugira ngo tubashe kubikora bidusaba kujya i Karuruma.  Abaturage ba Nyakariro mu Karere ka Rwamagana ndetse n abo mu Murenge wa Ruhuha mu Karere ka Bugesera na bo bakunze kwinubira kugira ihuzanzira mu itumanaho ricikagurika bituma bagorwa no gutumanaho  na telefone ngendanwa. Mu mwaka wa 2021, Urwego rw Igihugu rushinzwe inzego zimwe z imirimo ifitiye igihugu akamaro (RURA), rwasabye kompanyi z itumanaho gukemura ibibazo byose bigaragara mu itumanaho kubera ko abaturage bari bamaze imyaka myinshi bagaragaza ko guhamagara no gukoresha interineti bigoranye cyane. Hakenewe iminara irenga 2000 Mu kwakira kwa 2023, Minisitiri w Ikoranabuhanga na Inovasiyo Ingabire Paula yatangaje ko u Rwanda rukeneye iminara irenga ibihumbi 2 kugira ikibazo cy ihuzanzira rya interineti mu gihugu hose gikemuke. Kugeza ubu iminara igera ku bihumbi 2,800 yamaze gushingwa hirya no hino mu gihugu. Minisitiri Paula yavuze ko hakenewe nibura miliyoni 30 z amadolari y Amerika (arenga miliyari 30 z amafaranga y u Rwanda) mu kwagura imiyoboro ya interineti kuri site 300 zatoranyijwe hirya no hino mu gihugu. Ikigo gishinzwe ikoreshwa rya telefone ngendanwa ku Isi kigaragaza ko u Rwanda ruri ku kigero cya 61,5 by ibikorwa remezo bikenewe ku gukwirakwiza interineti, mu gihe  abaturage 30.3 %  ari bo babona iyo interineti mu buryo bworoshye kandi buhendutse ndetse na 42.1% by abaguzi bashobora kuyibona. Kugeze ubu abaturage bashobora kugerwaho na interineti mu Rwanda hose ni 60.6%. Abakoresha telefone ngendanwa ni 81,4%.
link192: Ikigo cy u Rwanda gishinzwe Ikoranabuhanga mu Itumanaho n Isakazabumenyi (RISA) cyasinyanye amasezerano y ubufatanye n Ikigo cya Saudi Arabia gishinzwe Ikoranabuhanga, agamije guteza imbere ikoranabuhanga mu bihugu byombi. Ni amasezerano yashyizweho umukono ubwo habaga Inama ya 3 y Inteko Rusange y Umuryango w Ubutwererane mu by Ikoranabuhanga (DCO), i Manama mu Bwami bwa Bahrain. Ikigo RISA kibona ayo masezerano nk intambwe ikomeye mu bufatanye bw u Rwanda na Saudi Arabia bugamije impinduramatwara mu by ikoranabuhanga. Iyi nama yasoje ku wa Gatatu tariki ya 31 Mutarama 2024 hatangizwa gahunda zitandukanye mu by ikoranabuhanga hagati y ibihugu bihuriye muri uwo Muryango. Yayobowe na Minisitiri w Ubwikorezi n Ikoranabuhanga mu Bwami bwa Bahrain Mohamed bin Thamir Al Kaabi, ikaba yitabiriwe n intumwa z ibihugu 16 biburiye muri uyu Muryango harimo n u Rwanda. Ibyo bihugu bifite Umusaruro Mbumbe (GDP) ukomatanyije wa tiriyari 3.5 z amadolari y Amerika, byaganiriye ku guteza imbere isoko ryambukiranya imipaka, agaciro k amakuru abikwa mu buryo bw ikoranabuhanga, ubukungu bwa muntu burambye bwifashisha ikoranabuhanga ndetse n ubutwererane mpuzamahanga butanga umusaruro muri urwo rwego. Baganiriye kandi ku iterambere ry ubucuruzi bwifashisha ikoranabuhanga, ishoramari no guhanga imirimo byose bigamije kwihutisha icyerekezo cy iterambere rishingiye ku ikoranabuhanga. U Rwanda n ibindi bihugu bihuriye muri uwo Muryango byongeye gushimangira ukwiyemeza kwa byo mu kubaka no gushyigikira imikorere ya DCO, bizirikana ko byose bihuriye ku ntego y iterambere rishingiye ku ikoranabuhanga. Abahagarariye ibihugu byabo bashimangiye akamaro k ubutwererane mpuzamahanga mu by ikoranabuhanga no kwihutisha iterambere rirambye kandi ritagira n umwe riheza ku Isi yose. Nanone kandi ibihugu bihuriye muri uyu Muryango byiyemeje gukumira ko icyuho mu mikoreshereze y ikoranabuhanga cyaba imbigamizi aho kubaka ikiraro hagati y abakire n abakene ngo bose baryoherwe n amahirwe ritanga. Ibyo bihugu bisanga kugira ngo Ikoranabuhanga rifashe mu rugendo rwo kugera ku Ntego z Iterambere Rirambye (SDGs) bisaba ubutwererane budacogora bw inzego zishinzwe kwimakaza ikoranabuhanga muri buri gihugu, mu bigo by ubucuruzi no hagati y abantu ubwabo. Ibihugu bihuriye muri uyu Muryango kandi byatangije gahunda nshya yo kubaka Ibigo by Icyitegererezo by Ikiranabuhanga ry Ubwenge Muntu Buhangano (DCO GenAI Center of Excellence Initiative) bizajyana no kubihuza hifashishijwe ikoranabuhanga rigezweho. Izindi gahunda zatangajwe mu kwimakaza ubutwererane mu by ikoranabuhanga harimo iyo Gushinga Ambasade y Amakuru abikwa ku Ikoranabuhanga, ndetse na Gahunda yimakaza ubusugire n ubuziranenge bw umutungo mu by ubwenge buri kuri murandasi. Nanone kandi Inteko Rusange ya DCO yatangarijwemo abemerewe guhagararira ibihugu byabo n indorerezi 17 baturutse mu nzego n ibihugu bitandukanye, byose bishimangira ukwiyemeza mu kwimakaza ubutwererane mu by ikoranabuhanga, no kuziba icyuho mu mikoreshereze yaryo. Umunyamabanga Mukuru wa DCO Deemah AlYahya, yashimiye Guverinoma ya Bahrain yakiriye inama y Inteko Rusange y uyu mwaka n ibihugu byayitabiriye bikaba byaranataze inkunga ishoboka mu mwaka wose. Yavuze ko uyu munsi hakenewe ubufatanye n ubutwererane buhamye mu bafatanyabikorwa bose, mu gihe Isi ihanganye n ubusumbane bushingiye ku ikoranabuhanga rigezweho nka AI. Yagize ati:  Mu bufatanye, dushobora guharanira ko iterambere nta n umwe riheza kandi rikaba rirambye tubihisemo, atari amahirwe. Dufite ibisabwa n impano byadufasha kubaka ikiraro kiziba icyuho cy ubusumbane mu ikoranabuhanga, duharura amayira y aho nta n umwe usigara inyuma.  Umuryango DCO washinzwe mu mwaka wa 2020, kuri ubu uhuriza hamwe Minisiteri z Ikoranabuhanga n Itumanaho zo mu bihugu 16 ari byo Bahrain, Bangladesh, Cyprus, Djibouti, Gambia, Ghana, Greece, Ubwami bwa Yorodaniya, Kuwait, Morocco, Nigeria, Oman, Pakistan, Qatar, u Rwanda, na Saudi Arabia. Ni Umuryango wibanda ku guteza imbere urubyiruko, abagore na ba rwiyemezamirimo basogongezwa ku mbaraga zo kwihutisha iterambere ry ubukungu bushingiye ku ikoranabuhanga. Biteganyijwe ko Inteko Rusange y Umwaka utaha izabera mu Bwami bwa Hashemite bwa Yirodaniya muri Gashyantare 2025, nk Igihugu cyahawe kuyobora uyu Muryango muri uyu mwaka.
link193: Leta y u Rwanda na Leta Zunze Ubumwe z Abarabu (UAE) byashyize umukono ku masezerano yimakaza iterambere ry ikoranabuhanga ry ubwenge muntu buhangano (Artificial Intelligence/AI), hagamijwe kuziba icyuho hagati y iryo koranabuhanga n ubukungu bw Isi. Amasezerano yashyizweho umukono ku wa Kane tariki ya 18 Mutarama 2024, mu Nama ngarukamwaka y Ihuriro Mpuzamahanga ry Ubukungu (WEF) iteraniye i Davos mu Busuwisi ku nshuro ya 54. Yashyizweho umukono muri gahunda yatangijwe n amashami y Ikigo gishinzwe Impinduramatwara ya Kane mu Bukungu mu Rwanda (C4IR Rwanda) ndetse no muri UAE (C4IR UAE). C4IR ni ikigo gikorera mu bihugu bitandukanye, kikaba kigira uruhare rukomeye cyane mu kwimakaza iterambere ry ikoranabuhanga rigezweho nk irikoresha ubwenge muntu butari karemano, ubumenyi bwa mudasobwa mu guteganya ibizaba, gukoresha no guhererekanya ifaranga ry ikoranabuhanga (blockchain) n imitungo ibitswe kuri ryo, ndetse no gusakaza ibikoresho by ikoranabuhanga bikenera internet (IoT). Biteganyijwe ko iyo gahunda yatangijwe hagati y u Rwanda na UAE izakomeza kwiyungaho andi mashami ya C4IR mu bice bitandukanye by Isi, ikaba izagira uruhare mu guhererekanya ubumenyi n ubunararibonye hagati y abakoresha AI ku Isi. Umuryango w abakoresha iryo koranabuhanga ry ubwenge butari karemano ntibazasangira ubunararibonye gusa ahubwo bazanafatanya mu gushaka ibisubizo by imbogamizi politiki yimakaza iryo koranabuhanga ihura na zo. Ubwo bufatanye bwitezweho kwihutisha no kuyobora icyerekezo cy ahazaza ha AI mu bukungu n imibereho y abatuye Isi hagamijwe kubaka ibiramba. Minisitiri w Ikoranabuhanga na Inovasiyo Ingabire M. Paula, yagaragaje ko u Rwanda rwishimiye kuba mu batangije iyo gahunda y ubufatanye bwimakaza iterambere ry ikoranabuhanga ry ubwenge muntu butari karemano. Yagize ati:  Tunejejwe cyane no kuba muri gahunda y ubufatanye na bagenzi bacu ba UAE bwimakaza AI. U Rwanda rwiyemeje kubyaza umusaruro iryo koranabuhanga mu kuyobora no kwihutisha iterambere ridaheza, kwimakaza umuryango w abarikoresha bashaka ibisubizo by ingorane duhura na zo muri iki gihe.  Yakomeje agira ati:  Binyuze mu bufatanye no gusangira ubumenyi n ubunararibonye, turaharanira kuba intangarugero mu guhanga udushya no guhindura icyerekezo cya AI, tukayigira igikoresho kidaheza kandi cyuje ubunyamwuga gitanga inyungu kuri bose.  Khalfan Belhoul, Umuyobozi w Umuryango Dubai Future Foundation, na we yongeyeho ko iyo gahunda y ubufatanye hagati y ibigo biharanira impinduramatwara ya kane mu bukungu izagira uruhare mu guhuza umuryango w abakoresha AI mu gukemura ibibazo iryo koranabuhanga rihura na byo. Yagize ati:  Bazakorana mu gushyiraho politiki nshya n amategeko byihutisha iterambere ry ikoranabuhanga. Iyo gahunda mpuzamahanga izibanda cyane ku guhererekanya ubumenyi binyuze mu mikoranire ya C4IR ku Isi yose.  Izafasha guhuriza hamwe ubumenyi bwungutswe hatunganywa imishinga ya AI ku Isi yose mu kwihutisha iterambere no kurushaho gutanga umusaruro.  Iyo gahunda kandi izategurirwamo inama zihariye zitandukanye zigamije ku kwigira hamwe imbogamizi n amahirwe birangwa muri AI. Ibyo biganiro bizakorwa mu buryo bw ubushakashatsi, gukoresha sisitemu za AI, no guhanga ibishya, hibandwa cyane ku bunararibonye bwa buri wese utanga umusanzu muri C4IR. Ubwo buryo buharanira ko buri kiganiro, inama na gahunda z ubufatanye biba bisubiza ibibazo by abahuriye muri iyo gahunda. Biteganyijwe kandi ko hazajya hategurwa amahugurwa ahuriweho mu gushishikariza ibihugu guhanga udushya muri applications za AI, kwimakaza imitekerereze mishya, no gushaka ibisubizo byifashisha ikoranabuhanga rigezweho. Nanone kandi amahugurwa azafasha kureba ku bunyamwuga, imiterere y ubuyobozi ndetse na Politiki zitandukanye ziyobora imikoreshereze ya AI. Ni amahugurwa kandi azafasha mu gushyiraho ingamba butegura politiki mpuzamahanga mu guharanira imikoreshereze n imikorere ya AI yubahiriza amategeko kandi itagira ibyo yangiza. Biteganyijwe kandi ko ubwo bufatanye buzagira uruhare mu gutegura imishinga mishya ihindura imibereho y abatuye Isi binyuze mu guhanga imirimo no kwagura amahirwe yo kugira uruhare mu nama mpuzamahanga ziga ku iterambere rya AI.
link194: Umugabo witwa Habimana Fabrice w Imyaka 28 utuye mu Karere ka Muhanga mu Murenge wa Shyogwe, mu Kagali ka Mubuga usanzwe akora imishinga y Ikoranabuhanga agamije gushaka ibisubizo by ibibazo bitandukanye aravuga ko  Zero Absenteism Software  yayikoze agamije kugabanya ibibazo birimo umubare w abana bata ishuri. Mu kiganiro yahaye Imvaho Nshya avuga ko afite inyota yo gukora byinshi akoresheje ikoranabuhanga kandi rigatanga akazi ku bakiri bato ari nako rizana igisubizo mu bibazo bitandukanye bibangamiye imibereho myiza y Abaturage. Avuga ko gahunda ya  Zero Absentism Software  izafasha abayobozi bomu Nzego z ibanze zizaba zifite uburenganzira bwo kumenya niba umwana wagombaga kujya ku ishuri yagiyeyo no kumenya impamvu atajya ku ishuri. Habimana ati:  Iyi Software izasha abayobozi bo mu Nzego z ibanze zizagira uburenganzira bwo kumenya niba umwana wagombaga kujya ku ishuri yagezeyo akaba yize ndetse no kumenya n impamvu atagiye kwiga . Akomeza avuga ko iri koranabuhanga rizaba rifite umwihariko ko rizajya rigaragaza umubare w Abanyeshuri bitabiriye ishuri mu Murenge, mu Karere ndetse no ku rwego rw Igihugu bakamenya amakuru azafasha gukurikirana neza abatageze ku ishuri. Yagize Ati Iri koranabuhanga nakoze rizaba rifite umwihariko wuko rizajya rigaragaza umubare w abanyeshuri bitabiriye ishuri ku rwego rw Umudugudu, Akagali, Umurenge, Akarere ndetse na Minisiteri y Uburezi bakajya bamenya neza uko abana bitabiriye ishuri kuri uwo munsi mu gihugu cyose . Yongeyeho ko atekereza gukora iyi  Software  yatekereje cyane ku mibare y abanyeshuri batiga neza bagata ishuri bisubiza inyuma Ireme ry Uburezi abenshi bavuga ko rigenda ritakara cyane. Yagize ati:  Njya gutekereza gukora iri koranabuhanga natekereje ku Ireme ry Uburezi kuko Minisiteri yagiye igaragaza ko guta ishuri no kutiga bisubiza inyuma iri reme ry uburezi kuko umwana yamaze iminsi atabashije kwigira hamwe . Habimana Fabrice ubusanzwe yize amashuri y Ikiciro cya kabiri cya Kaminuza mu gihugu cya Malaysia ari naho yigiye ibijyanye n iri koranabuhanga, yize ibijyanye no gukora amashanyarazi, arimo gukora nubwo mu mashuri yisumbuye. Hamimana yanabashije gushyiraho uburyo bwo gusinya ku bakozi b Ibigo bitandukanye kandi bikora neza kuko umukoresha amenya neza igihe umukozi yaziye ku kazi n Igihe umukozi yakaviriyemo. Yatangarije Imvaho Nshya ko kugera ubu afite ibigo bisaga ibihumbi 2 byamaze guhabwa uburyo bugezweho bwo kumenyesha isaha ya mwalimu urimo kwigisha isomo ko mminota yagenewe umwarimu irangiye, bityo bikarinda umunyeshuri gutakaza iminota ajya kuvuza icyuma abenshi bazi nka  Kadende  kandi abandi barimo kwiga. Yatanze umukoro ku rubyiruko rusanzwe rufite ibitekerezo byo kuzamura impano zabo mu mishinga y ikoranabuhanga ko bakwiye gukomeza kuzamura impano zabo mu ikoranabuhanga. Mu mibare igaragazwa na Minisiteri y Uburezi mu Rwanda igaragaza ko abana bafite imyaka iri hagati 7-12 bagabanyutse bava kuri 98.9% muri 2020-2021 bagera kuri 95,2% mu mwaka wa 2021-2022. Gusa ubu bushakashatsi kandi bwerekanye ko urebye ku bana bitabira ishuri barenga 141,5% bivuze ko hari abana baje ku ishuri batarageza imyaka cyangwa bakaza barengeje imyaka yo kujya ku ishuli. Iyi raporo kandi igaragaza ko mu mwaka wa 2019 -2020 mu mashuri abanza 9,5% bari barataye ishuri naho mu mwaka wa 2020-2021 abagera ku 7,1% nabo bataye ishuri. Mu mashuri yisumbuye mu mwaka wa 2019-2020 abasaga 10,3% bataye ishuri naho mu mwaka wa 2020-2021 abagera ku 9,2% bataye ishuri ariko muri rusange abahungu ni bo benshi bataye ishuri. Muri Raporo yashyizwe hanze n Ishami ry Umuryango w Abibumbye rishinzwe Uburezi, Ubumenyi n Umuco (UNESCO)rigaragaza ko mu mwaka wa 2022 abana bari hagati y imyaka 6-18 bagera kuri miliyoni 244 batari bari ku ishuri cyangwa ngo babe bari mu kazi ndetse abenshi basangwa mu bihugu byo munsi y Ubutayu bwa Sahara n iyo Hagati no mu Majyepfo y Aziya ari natwo dufite umubare mwinshi.
link195: Ubuyobozi bwa Koperative Umwalimu SACCO bwemeje ko muri uyu mwaka wa 2024 bugiye kurushaho kunoza ikoranabuhanga ryoroshya serivisi, by umwihariko Mobile Banking ifasha abarimu kubitsa, kubikuza, gusaba inguzanyo n ibindi bitabasabye kujya ku mashami abegereye. Ubwo buyobozi buvuga ko mu bikorwa by ibanze bizibandwaho muri uyu mwaka wa 2024, ari ugukoresha ikoranabuhanga kuko rizagabanya ingendo abarimu bakoraga bajya gushakisha serivisi. Nubwo hari serivisi zimwe na zimwe sisanzwe zitangwa hifashishijwe ikoranabuhanga, ubuyobozi bw iyo Koperative bwemeza ko hari ahakigaragara icyuho by umwihariko muri sisitemu ya Mobile Banking idakora neza. Uwambaje Laurence, Umuyobozi Mukuru wa Koperative Umwalimu SACCO, avuga ko bagiye kurushaho kunoza iryo koranabuhanga bagamije kugabanya ingendo mwarimu akora ajya gusaba serivisi z imari. Ati:  Igikorwa cyo kwibandwaho ni uburyo bwo gutanga serivisi tugabanya ikiguzi bisaba mwarimu kugira ngo akore urugendo rugera kuri serivisi z imari tumuha. Aha rero dushyira imbaraga cyane mu gukoresha uburyo bugezweho, aho kugira ngo umwarimu aze ku ishami abe yakwiha serivisi wenyine.  Yakomeje agira ati:  Twashyizeho ko tuzakomeza kwibanda cyane kuri ibyo bikorwa bituma serivisi zegera abanyamuryango, kandi noneho bakabyikorera bitabasabye kuza ku ishami, bakinjira muri sisitemu zacu ako kanya tugahita tubona igikozwe.  Yongeyeho ko aho zimwe muri sisitemu z ikoranabuhanga zitakoraga neza hazibandwa mu kuzitunganya no kurushaho kuzongerera ubushobozi. Ati:  Hamaze iminsi havugwa ko Mobile Banking idakora, neza ubu twashyizeho ko tuzibanda cyane mu kuyitunganya igakora neza kugira ngo abanyamuryango babone serivisi zihuse. Twashyizeho sisitemu yo gusaba inguzanyo hifashishijwe ikoranabuhanga, aho guca kuri Email twashyizeho sisitemu izajya ikora isesengura ry inguzanyo kugira ngo umunyamuryango abone amakuru y aho inguzanyo igeze ndetse n ibibura akabyohereza atiriwe aza ku ishami.  Kugeza ubu Koperative Umwalimu SACCO ifite amashami 30, kandi ifite imikoranire n Umurenge SACCO aho kuri ubu abarimu basigaye basabira serivisi ahaboroheye.
link196: Mu bice bimwe na bimwe by Umujyi wa Kigali no mu Turere dutandukanye tw Intara y Iburasirazuba, abaturage batangiye gukoresha amavomo babona amazi bakojeje ikarita kuri mubazi y ikoranabuhanga ikoresha amashanyarazi n ihuzanzira rya internet. Umuturage ashobora kubonera amazi isaha yose abishakiye adategereje ko hari uwaza kumufungurira amazi. Icyo asabwa gusa ni ugukoza ikarita kuri mubazi, igahita imurekurira litiro 20 z amazi yishyura igiceri cya 20 cy amafaranga y u Rwanda. Ubuyobozi bw Ikigo cy Igihugu gishinzwe gukwirakwiza Amazi, Isuku n Isukura (WASAC), buvuga ko ubu buryo bwatangiriye ku mavomo rusange 56 aherereye mu bice bitandukanye by i Kigali no mu Turere twa Kayonza, Rwamagana, Gatsibo na Nyagatare. Bamwe mu baturage batuye mu Mujyi wa Kayonza bakoresha ayo mavomo rusange, bavuga ko kuvoma bakoresheje ikoranabuhanga byabakuriyeho inzitizi zirimo kuzinduka bakabura uvomesha n umubyigano. Aba baturage bavuga ko iri koranabuhanga ritarabageraho bari bafite imbogamizi n ibibazo byo kutabonera amazi meza igihe cyose bayashakiye bitewe n uko ushinzwe kuvomesha adahari gusa. Gisubizo Jean Claude ukoresha ivomo rusange riri mu Kagari ka Nyagatovu mu Murenge wa Mukarange, avuga ko iryo koranabuhanga ryabakijije inkomati ndetse n amazi yarabahendukiye kuko ntayo bagipfusha ubusa. Yagize ati:  Izi mubazi zitaraza byadusabaga gutegereza uvomesha ugasanga tubaye benshi bityo ugasanga habayeho kubyigana tuyarwanira. Ariko ubu aho ubu buryo bw ikoranabuhanga buziye iyo watinze mu kazi ugataha bugorobye ntutegereza ushinzwe kuvoma ngo agufungurire cyangwa mu gitondo uzindutse. Imirongo yaragabanyutse ntabwo uza ngo utegereze kuko dufite amakarita dukoresha tuvoma batiriwe baza kukuvomera.  Mahatane Theoneste nawe yagize ati:  Njye hari igihe mva mu kazi saa yine z ijoro nkaza kuvoma hano. Nkubu mvomye amajerekani atanu, ubu hagiye igiceri cy ijana. Uvomesha iyo yabaga adahari byadusabaga kumurindira ariko ubu aho nshakira kugaruka ndaza ntikandagira nta kibazo.  Kantarama Viviane ashinzwe rimwe muri ayo mavomo rusange riri mu Mujyi wa Kayonza mu Kagari ka Bwiza, asobanura ko mbere batarakoresha ikoranabuhanga ryo kuvoma yasigaga imirimo mu rugo akajya kuvomesha ndetse agahura n igihombo cyaterwaga n amazi yangirikaga. Yagize ati:  Iyo nabaga naje kuvomesha nasigaga imirimo mu rugo ugasanga mu rugo hari imirimo yangirika kuko umwanya wose nabaga ndi ku ivomero mvomesha, ariko ubu baraza bakavoma batantegereje nanjye nkajya mu mirimo yanjye ntawunzinduye cyangwa ngo ambyutse nageze mu buriri.  Yakomeje avuga ko mbere yahuraga n ibihombo by amazi yamenekaga ariko ngo ubu ntibigishoboka kuko umuntu avoma amazi asabye. Ati:  Uburyo bwo kuvoma busanzwe bwatumaga mpura n igihombo kuko amazi yamenekaga, ni njye wayishyuraga aho iyo bambariraga wasangaga ngeza nko mu mafaranga 5,000 by amazi yamenetse, ariko kuko ikarita iba iregeye bijyanye na buri jerekani ntibigikunda.  Mukiza Anaclet, Umukozi w Ishami rya WASAC rya Kayonza, yavuze ko ubu buryo bwo gukoresha mubazi bumaze imyaka ibiri, bukaba bukiri mu igeregeza aho bwatangirijwe kandi bukomeje gutanga umusaruro. Yavuze ko kugira ngo buri vomo rikoresha ikoranabuhanga rigezweho ryubakwe ritwara ingengo y imari ya miliyoni imwe y amafaranga y u Rwanda kandi rikajyana n ibindi bikorwa remezo birimo umuriro w amashanyarazi n ihuzanzira rya internet. Mukiza yavuze ko mu gihe Guverinoma y u Rwanda yihaye intego yo kwegereza amazi meza abaturage bose, hari na gahunda yo kurushaho kwagura iryo koranabuhanga mu tundi Turere. Yagize ati:  Igerageza ryatweretse ko ari ryiza yaba mu Ntara no mu Mujyi wa Kigali kandi tuzagenda twongera uko ubushobozi buzajya buboneka kuko twasanze bifasha abaturage benshi mu buryo bwihuse kandi bunoze. Gusa ariko ubu buryo burahenze kuko busaba kuba ibikorwa remezo by umuriro na  network  biba bikenewe ariko tugenda buhororo buhoro.  Mu gihe cy imyaka ibiri, umushinga wo gukoresha ikoranabuhanga rya mubazi ku mavomo rusange umaze ugeragezwa, mu Karere ka Kayonza umaze kugezwa ku mavomo umunani. Mubazi ikoreshwa na WASAC, ni ikoranabuhanga ryatumye gahunda yo kuvoma amasaha 24/24 ishoboka. Abaturage bavuga ko imbogamizi ikiri aho ayo mavomo yashyizwe ari iyo kuba amakarita yifashishwa afitwe n abantu bakeya, dore ko ikarita nta kiguzi isaba uretse kuba ufite irangamuntu na telefoni. Udafite ikarita ategereza uyifite akamukorezaho na we akabona kuvoma.
link197: Ni ngombwa ko ababyeyi bakurikirana bakagenzura ibyo abana babo bakurikira ku ikoranabuhanga, kugira ngo bamenye niba ari ibibubaka cyangwa niba ari ibibasenya, cyane cyane mu minsi mikuru isoza umwaka. Minisitiri w Ikoranabuhanga na Inovasiyo, Ingabire Musoni Paula, avuga ko mu Minsi Mikuru ya Noheli n Ubunani usanga ababyeyi ari bwo baba bashaka kuruhuka, akabasaba kugenera abana ibyo bareba mu buryo bw ikoranabuhanga. Yagize ati:  Muri iyi Minsi Mikuru ababyeyi bagomba kwibuka kugenzura uko abana babo bakoresha ibikoresho by ikoranabuhanga kuko n abakoreraho ibyaha baba biyongereye. Ababyeyi kandi bashobora no kugena ibyo abana bareba n ibyo batareba ku ikoranabuhanga mu rwego rwo kubarinda.  Yongeyeho ati:  Mu buzima busanzwe umubyeyi akenshi ava ku kazi ananiwe yabona weekend agashaka kuruhuka noneho cya gihe akeneye kuruhuka abana ugasanga ubarekuriye bya bikoresho by ikoranabuhanga kugira ngo ubarangaze ho gato nawe ubone akanya ko kuruhuka. Ariko ikibazo kivamo ni uko urimo kuruhuka ntuba uzi ibyo bari bukubitane na byo kuri iryo koranabuhanga cyangwa bya bikoresho wabahaye.  Minisitiri Musoni yakomeje asobanura ko uko ikoranabuhanga ritera imbere, ubu hari uburyo bwo kugena icyo umwana yareba. Ati:  Hari ibintu bibiri navuga, icya mbere iyo umubyeyi atanze ibikoresho by ikoranabuhanga, muri iyi minsi hari n uburyo bwo kugena ibyo umwana ashobora kureba bijyanye n imyaka ye, ibyo rero biba bisaba ko n umubyeyi abishyiramo imbaraga akavuga ati niba mfite umwana w imyaka 6 cyangwa 8 niba muhaye telefone cyangwa mushyiriyeho televiziyo ni gute nagena gahunda naba mpari naba ntahari ibyo ashobora kuba yareba agakurikira akareba ibijyanye n imyaka ye.  Ababyeyi bajye bagenera abana akanya ko kuganira Ababyeyi kandi bakangurirwa kujya bagena umwanya wo kuganiriza abana bakamenya niba mu byo barebye harimo ibikeneye ubugororangingo. Ati:  Icya kabiri aho umubyeyi ahugukiye biba ari byiza kumenya ngo umwana yakurikiye iki n ubwo biba bijyanye n imyaka ye hari igihe baba bashyizemo inyigisho zitari ngombwa. Ni byiza ko umubaza ibyo yabonye, akakuganiriza akaba yagera no ku kitari ngombwa unamufashe kugira ngo amenye ibiri ukuri n ibiri ngombwa [ ]. Bisaba ko ababyeyi bashaka uwo mwanya ngo baganire n abana n igihe bashyiriweho ibyo bikoresho ngo barebe.  Minisitiri Ingabire yavuze kandi ko ari ngombwa kugena, kugira gahunda nk ababyeyi kugira ngo upangire umwana ibindi akora nko gukina umupira, koga, basketball ni ibintu n ubundi biri bumugirire akamaro ku buzima bwe ariko bitari butume yumva ko yicaye nta kintu afite cyo gukora . Kugira gahunda mu muryango na byo ni ngombwa, umwana akaba afite gahunda y ibikorwa. Yagize ati:  Ni ngombwa mukaba muzi ngo ku isaha iyi n iyi ikiri bukorwe ni iki, harakurikiraho iki, igihe nkeneye kuruhuka araba afite ibyo akora ariko bimufitiye akamaro nk umwana biri bugire n icyo bimwungura . Umwe mu babyeyi ufite abana bari mu kigero gitandukanye, akaba ari n umwarimu ufite umwana umwe wiga mu wa 4 w ayisumbuye n uw imyaka 4, yatangarije Imvaho Nshya ko batabyitagaho ahubwo wasangaga bareba bimwe kuri televiziyo. Kuba basangira ibyo bareba rimwe na rimwe ngo hari ubwo bashwanaga kuko baba badashaka kureba bimwe, ariko ko bagiye kuzareba uko babigenza kugira ngo abana bajye bareba ibibubaka.
link198: Guverinoma y u Rwanda, ibinyujije muri Minisiteri y Ikoranabuhanga no guhanga Ibishya (MINICT) na Minisiteri y Uburezi  (MINEDUC), yatangiye ubufatanye n Ikigo Ignite Power yo gukwirakwiza internet ikoresha ingufu z imirasire y izuba mu mashuri yo mu bice by icyaro bitandukanye mu gihugu. Ignite Power ni ikigo Mpuzamahanga gitanga ibisubizo bishingiye ku ngufu zituruka ku mirasire y izuba mu miryango ikennye kurusha iyindi muri Afurika yo munsi y Ubutayu bwa Sahara,  giheruka gutsindira igihembo mpuzamahanga cyiswe Zayed Award cy uyu mwaka wa 2023. Ubufatanye bwatangiye hagati ya Leta y u Rwanda n icyo kigo bugamije kugeza internet ku bigo by amashuri biri mu byaro bya kure aho bigoye kugeza umuriro w amashanyarazi afatiye ku muyoboro mugari. Minisitiri w Ikoranabuhanga no guhanga Ibishya Ingabire Musoni Paula, yagize ati:  Ubu bufatanye busobanuye ukwiyemeza kwacu ko guharanira ko buri muturage, by umwihariko abanyeshuri, abona amahirwe angana n ay abandi muri iyi Si ikomeje gutera imbere mu ikoranabuhanga rigezweho.  Iyi gahunda yitezweho gufasha amashuri yo mu Rwanda kubona ibikoresho bigezweho by ikoranabuhanga birimo anteni za LinX zikurura internet itangwa n ibyogajuru, bigatuma ibigo by amashuri bibona internet inyaruka ku giciro gito aho byaba biherereye hose. Nubwo hari intambwe ikomeye imaze guterwa mu rwego rw uburezi mu Rwanda, Leta y u Rwanda ivuga ko hakiri amashuri yo mu byaro bya kure ataragerwaho n umuriro w amashanyarazi ndetse n ibikorwa remezo bya internet, bityo abanyeshuri bakagorwa no kugera ku ikoranabuhanga ribafasha kubyaza umusaruro amahirwe ya internet. Ubwo bufatanye bwitezweho kuba igisubizo kirambye mu kuziba icyuho cyarangwaga mu rugamba rwo guharanira kugeza uburezi bungana kuri bose binyuze mu kubaha ibikorwa remezo by ibanze birimo n ihuzanzira rya internet. Minisitiri Ingabire yakomeje agira ati:  Tunejejwe no gutangiza ubu bufatanye n ikigo cy abikorera cy intangarugero nka Ignite Power. Kugeza internet kuri bose mu burezi ni ingenzi cyane kugira ngo tugere ku ntego yo kubaka sosiyete ishingiye ku bumenyi.  Ignite Power itangiye ubwo bufatanye mu gihe yari imaze no kwigaragaza mu Rwanda nk ikigo gishoboye gukwirakwiza ingufu kuko imaze kuzigeza ku baturage barenga miliyoni mu bice bitandukanye by Igihugu aho bamaze kugezwaho ibikoresho by imirasire bigezweho kandi bikora mu buryo burambye. Ikoranabuhanga rya LinX solution, rigiye kugezwa mu mashuri rikoresha imirasire y izuba ku kigero cya 100%, bikaba ari byo bizoroshya kuba zashyirwa mu mashuri ataragezwamo amashanyarazi asanzwe, bikaba bijyanye na gahunda y Igihugu yo kugera ku Ntego z Iterambere rirambye z Umuryango w Abibumbye (UNSDGs). Yariv Cohen, Umuyobozi Mukuru wa Ignite Power, yashimangiye ko kugeza ibikorwa remezo by ibanze ku bantu bose ari ingenzi cyane, ati:  Ihuzanzira rya internet ryahindutse igikorwa remezo shingiro n uburenganzira bwa muntu mu Isi ya none. Tunejejwe gukorana na Guverinoma y u Rwanda mu guharurira inzira ahazaza hatagira n umwe hasigaza inyuma, aho u Rwanda ruyoboye impinduka no mu bindi bihugu by Afurika.  Cohen yakomeje agira ati:  Ibisubizo byacu byifashisha ingufu z imirasire y izuba 100% byihutisha ikwizwa ry ikoranabuhanga kandi bikanashimangira ukwiyemeza kwacu mu gushyigikira ibiramba. Iyi gahunda irashyira ibuye ry ifatizo ku iterambere ridaheza kandi rirambye mu Rwanda no hanze.
link199: Minisiteri y Uburezi ivuga ko uburezi bw u Rwanda buri gutera intambwe mu rugendo rwo gukoresha ikoranabuhanga, aho  amashuri yose yahawe internet ageze kuri 60%, ndetse bikaba byitezwe ko umwaka wa 2024 uzarangira amashuri yose afite internet. Ni ibyagarutsweho na Minisitiri w Uburezi Twagirayezu Gaspard mu nama y iminsi itatu yitwa  Innovation Africa Summit  iteraniye i Kigali uhereye kuri uyu wa 30 Ukwakira. Iyi nama ihurijwemo Abaminisitiri b Uburezi b Afurika n abafatanyabikorwa mu by ikoranabuhanga, aho bari kurebera hamwe uko ikoranabuhanga ryakemura ibibazo bikigaragara mu burezi bw Afurika. Minisitiri Twagirayezu Gaspard avuga ko u Rwanda rugeze kuri 60% ruha amashuri internet mu rwego rwo kwirinda gusigara inyuma mu gukoresha ikoranabuhanga. Ati:  Mu Rwanda twashyize imbaraga mu gushyiraho umuyoboro wo guha amashuri yose internet ubu tugeze hafi 60%, ariko dufite intego ko 2024 izarangira amashuri yose afite internet. Turi kongera ibikoresho by ikoranabuhanga haba ari mudasobwa cyangwa telefone abarimu bakoresha no kugira amasomo yigishwa hakoreshejwe ikoranabuhanga.  Yongeyeho ko abarimu bakora amahugurwa mu rwego rwo kumenya gukoresha ikoranabuhanga. Hagaragajwe ibibazo bikibangamiye uburezi bw Afurika, n uburyo byakemuka hakoreshejwe ikoranabuhanga. Ati:  Ikoranabuhanga ryadufasha gukemura ibibazo byo mu burezi kuko twarebeye hamwe akamaro ko gukora integanyanyigisho nziza zireba ku bibazo dufite tutirengagije n uburyo Afurika yatezwa imbere binyuze mu burezi . Minisitiri w Uburezi wa Afurika y Epfo Dr Reginah Mhaule, avuga ko igihugu cye cyigira ku Rwanda uko bakoresha ikoranabuhanga mu burezi, kandi nubwo COVID-19 yaje ari icyorezo ariko yeretse Afurika ko kwiga hakoreshejwe ikoranabuhanga bishoboka. Ati:  Rimwe na rimwe abantu batekereza ko turi imbere mu by ikoranabuhanga ariko u Rwanda na Kenya bo bateye imbere cyane. Tujya tuza no kubigiraho, rero dukwiye kuva mu byakera uburezi bukisanga mu Isi y ikoranabuhanga. Nubwo COVID-19 yaje ari icyorezo ariko yatweretse ko gukoresha ikoranabuhanga muri byose bishoboka.  Iyi nama ibaye ku nshuro ya 11 aho iba igamije kwigira hamwe insanganyamatsiko zitandukanye zirebana n iterambere ry uburezi.
link200: Guverinoma y u Rwanda yatangiye kureba ku mahirwe atandukanye ajyanye no kurushaho kubyaza umusaruro ikoreshwa ry indege nto zitagira abapilote (drones) mu rwego rwo guharanira iterambere rigendanye n ibyo u Rwanda rwiyemeje mu kwimakaza ikoranabuhanga rigezweho. Ni mu gihe indege nto zitagira abapilote zikomeje kubonwa nk umufasha ukomeye mu mitangire ya serivisi mu nzego zinyuranye uhereye ku rw ubuzima, umutekano, ibidukikije, ubuhinzi n ubworozi, umutekano, n izindi. Mu mwaka wa 2016 ni bwo indege nto zitagira abapilote zatangiye kwandika amateka akomeye mu Rwanda, zitwara amaraso yo gutabara indembe mu bitaro bitandukanye byo mu gihugu birimo n ibiherereye ahantu hagoranye kugera hifashishijwe inzira y ubutaka. Nyuma y imyaka mike drones zifashishijwe mu rugamba rwo guhangana na COVID-19, zifashishwa mu kugeza intanga ku borozi batandukanye mu gihugu, mu bikorwa byo kurwanya malariya aho zifashishwa mu gutera imiti mu bishanga, gusuzuma imiterere y ubutaka no gutera imiti mu myaka n ibindi. Muri uku kwezi, Minisitiri w Ibidukikije Dr Mujawamariya Jeanne d Arc, yatangarije Abasenateri ko izo drones zigiye kwifashishwa mu kugenzura abangiza ibidukikije. Mu nama iteraniye i Kigali kuri uyu wa Gatatu tariki ya 29 Ugushyingo, yiga ku kuteza imbere uruhererekane rw imikoreshereze ya drones mu Rwanda, Ingabire M. Paula Minisitiri w Ikoranabuhanga no guhanga Ibishya, yavuze ko abafatanyabikorwa batandukanye bahujwe no gutanga ibitegekerezo byo kurushaho kwimakaza ikoreshwa rya drones mu Rwanda. Yagize ati:  Uyu munsi ntabwo ari ibirori gusa; ni uguhuza ibitekerezo kugira ngo u Rwanda ruhagarare neza kandi rube intangarugero ku Isi yose mu guteza imbere ikoreshwa rya drones no guhanga udushya. Reka twubake umwuka w ubufatanye, guhanga udushya, ndetse no gufata inshingano.  Iyo nama yitabiriwe n inzego zitandukanye z abafatanyabikorwa mu iterambere ry uruhererekane rw indege nto zitagira abapilote, abo bafatanyabikorwa bakaba barimo kurebera hamwe uko barushaho kwagura imikoranire igamije kurushaho kwimakaza iterambere rya drones hubahirizwa intego z u Rwanda mu iterambere ry ikoranabuhanga. Muri iyo nama kandi haramurikirwamo amahirwe anyuranye y imikoranire muri urwo rwego ndetse na gahunda nshya z imikoranire ishoboka mu gihe kizaza. Ikoranabuhanga rya drone rikomeje gutera imbere muri iyi myaka aho rikoreshwa mu nzego zinyuranye zaba iza Leta n iz abikorera mu bikorwa birimo gufata amashusho, kugeza ibicuruzwa ku bakiliya, gukusanya amakuru mu rwego rw umutekano n imicungire y ibiza, gukora ubushakashatsi, ubugenzuzi, ubwikorezi bw ibicuruzwa n ibindi bikoresho, kubahiriza amategeko, kwifashishwa mu iteganyagihe no kugenzura imipaka. Bivugwa ko hari n ubundi buryo bwinshi bukomeje gutegurwa kugira ngo bube bwakwifashishwa mu iterambere rya drones no kurushaho kuzibyaza umusaruro utanga inyungu zifatika ku baturage. Ubushakashatsi bwagaragaje ko ubucuruzi bushingiye ku ikoreshwa rya drone ku Isi buzaba bwinjije miliyari zisaga 500 z amadolari y Amerika kugeza mu mwaka wa 2030. Impuguke mu by ikoranabuhanga zigaragaza ko nta gushidikanya ko drone zizaba umusemburo w iterambere ry ikoranabuhanga n imitangire inoze ya serivi mu nzego zinyuranye.
link201: Kuri uyu wa Kane tariki 16 Ugushyingo 2023, Ikigo NALA cyashize ahagaragara uburyo buhendutse kandi bwizewe bwo kohereza amafaranga mu Rwanda. Ni nyuma yuko NALA yabonye uruhushya rutangwa na Banki Nkuru y u Rwanda (BNR) ruyemerera gukorera mu Rwanda. Igakora nk ikigo cy ubucuruzi cyemerewe gufasha mu kwishyurana no guhanahana amafaranga (Payment Service Provider). Uru ruhushya ni intambwe nziza mu gutuma NALA igeza ku banyarwanda uburyo bwayo bwizewe kuko amafaranga agera vuba ku wo yohererejwe kandi buhendutse bwo guhanahana amafaranga no kwishyurana binyuze mu ikoranabuhanga kuko nta kiguzi bisaba, bityo bigatuma u Rwanda ruba ihuriro ry ikoranabuhanga riteza imbere ubukungu. Umuyobozi ushinzwe ibikorwa muri NALA Nicolai Eddy yagize ati:  Kutwemerera guhuza ikoranabuhanga ryacu n amabanki ndetse n ibigo byifashisha ikoranabuhanga mu ihererekanya ry amafaranga, biratuma tubasha kugira uruhare mu gukemura bimwe mu bibazo abantu ku giti cyabo ndetse n ibigo by ubucuruzi bahura nabyo mu ihererekanya ry amafaranga, cyane cyane iyo hoherezwa amafaranga hanze y u Rwanda cyangwa ava mu mahanga aza mu Rwanda. Uru ruhushya ruratuma dutanga ibisubizo mu Rwanda; bisobanuye ko n urwego rwa serivisi zitangwa buri buzamuke ariko ibiciro bikamanuka.  Yongeyeho ati:  Twakoranye bya hafi na Banki Nkuru y u Rwanda kugira ngo tubashe kuzuza ibisabwa ngo duhabwe uru ruhushya. Nka NALA, dushimangiye intego yacu yo gukomeza ubufatanye n inzego z ubugenzuzi mu rwego rw ubukungu mu Rwanda ndetse n izindi nzego kugira ngo intego igihugu cyihaye zo kubaka ubukungu zigerweho.  Ubu buryo buzafasha ibigo by imari kwifashisha ikoranabuhanga (mobile money operators), harimo nko kwishyura ibyaguzwe, kwishyura amafaranga y ishuri ndetse no kwakira ubwishyu. NALA yatangiye gukorera mu Rwanda mu mwaka wa 2021 binyuze mu bufatanye n ibindi bigo. Ubufatanye bwashingiye cyane cyane ku gufasha kohereza amafaranga aturuka hanze ku makonti muri banki no mu bigo by ikoranabuhanga ryifashishwa telefoni (Mobile Money Wallets)Kuva muri uwo mwaka NALA yafashije ihererekanya ry amafaranga inshuro zirenga ibihumbi 10 inafasha ibihumbi by Abanyarwanda baba mu mahanga (Diaspora), koherereza imiryango yabo iri mu Rwanda amafaranga. Muri iri hererekanya, amafaranga arenga miliyari imwe y amafaranga y u Rwanda yohererejwe abantu baba mu Rwanda. Umuyobozi ushinzwe shoramari muri Rwanda Finance Limited Jean-Marie Kananura, yagize ati:  Ishyirwaho rya gahunda y ubukungu bushingiye ku ikoranabuhanga (fintech landscape) ndetse no gutuma u Rwanda ruba ihuriro ry ikoranabuhanga riteza imbere ubukungu bizafasha u Rwanda gukurura ishoramari muri uru rwego ndetse no guteza imbere serivisi z ubukungu zikenewe ngo u Rwanda rube koko ihuriro ry ubukungu ku Isi. Ikoranabuhanga kandi rinatuma serivisi z ubukungu zirushaho gutera imbere ndetse zikanagera kuri bose. U Rwanda rwihaye intego yo guteza imbere ubukungu atari gusa mu gihugu ahubwo no mu karere ndetse no muri Afurika yose muri rusange. lyi ntego ijya gusa n iyo NALA yihaye yo gufasha kongera amahirwe y iterambere ku banyafurika benshi aho bari hose ku Isi . Kuva mu mwaka WA 2021, NALA yafashishe ihererekanya ry amafaranga inshuro zirenga ibihumbi 10 ndetse ifasha ibihumbi by abanyarwanda baba mu mahanga (diaspora) koherereza imiryango yabo iri mu Rwanda amafaranga. Imibare ya Banki y Isi yerekana ko nibura kohereza amafranga muri Afurika bigusaba nibura kwishyura ikiguzi kingana na 9% by amafaranga wohereje. Ikindi cyagaragaye ni uko bumwe mu buryo busanzweho bwongeraho ikindi kiguzi kiba kitanditswe kugira ngo ubashe kohereza amafaranga; ibituma igiciro cy iyi serivisi kirushaho guhenda. NALA, ni sosiyete y ikoranabuhanga ryerekeye ku bukungu ikorera mu karere k Afurika y Iburasirazuba, ikomeje kwagura ibikorwa binyuze mu kwagura aho ikorera, kunoza ikoranabuhanga no guhanga udushya mu rwego w ubukungu. Kugeza ubu, ubu buryo bukoreshwa ku mafaranga aturutse mu Bwongereza, Leta zunze ubumwe za Amerika n Umuryango w Ubumwe bw u Burayi yoherezwa muri Tanzania, Kenya, Uganda, Ghana, Rwanda, Cameroon, Cote d Ivoire na Senegal. NYIRANEZA JUDITH
link202: Perezida wa Repubulika y u Rwanda Paul Kagame, yagaragaje uburyo ikintu gishya cyose kigeze mu muryango runaka kizana n impungenge zihariye, ashingiye ku kuba ikoranabuhanga ry ubwenge muntu buhangano (AI/artificial intelligence) rikomeje kuzamura impaka ku Isi yose ku kaga rishobora kuzakururira abatuye Isi. By umwihariko, Afurika ivugwaho kuba ari umugabane utaratera imbere mu by ikoranabuhanga ku buryo ukemangwa ku bushobozi bwayo mu kuba yiteguye kuryakira no kuribyaza umusaruro mu buryo bukwiriye. Perezida Kagame yavuze ko abantu badakwiye kwibanda gusa ku byago iryo koranabuhanga rizazana ahubwo bakabigereranya n inyungu rizana ku batuye Isi yose, maze hakabaho ubufatanye mu kugabanya ibyago byatekerejwe ari na ko hongerwa amahirwe iryo koranabuhanga rizana na yo. Yabiugarutseho kuri uyu wa Kabiri tariki ya 8 Ugushyingo, ubwo yifatanyaga na ba rwiyemezamirimo batandukanye bakorera ku cyicaro cy Ishami rya Norrsken muri Afurika giherereye mu Mujyi wa Kigali, mu gutangiza icyumweru cyahariwe ibikorwa bya Norrsken muri Afurika. Akaniwabo Vicky, Umuyobozi Mukuru w Ikigo Hence Technologies cyimakaza ikoranabuhanga ribika amakuru n iry ubwenge muntu buhangano (AI), yari abajije Perezida Kagame icyo avuga kuri iryo koranabuhanga rigezweho n icyo yabwira ba rwiyemezamirimo bakomeje guharanira ko Afurika na yo itazasigara inyuma. Yagize ati:  Buri kintu gishya mu muryango kizana n impungenge runaka. Reka dutangire tureba ikoranabuhanga muri rusange. Ikoranabuhanga rifite inyungu nyinshi cyane, rigeza abantu ku rwego rwisumbuye ku rwo bari bariho, ariko ni igenzi kugenda muri iyo nzira unatekereza ku nyungu mu buryo bwumvikana. Ariko nanone haza ingaruka z ibyo bikoresho n imitekerereze bishya ku muryango.  Yavuze ko impungenge zikwiye kurebwaho by umwihariko maze zigashyirwa ku munzani umwe n iryo koranabuhanga rikenewe ngo imibereho y abatuye Isi irusheho kunozwa. Ati:  Dukwiye kuba twibaza tuti ese iki kintu gishya gifite inyungu ku rwego rungana iki? Ariko se cyaba gifite ingorane runaka? Ni gute duharanira kuzikumira mu guharanira ko inyungu zirenga ibibazo bishobora kuvuka? Nta buryo ikigo cyangwa igihugu kimwe cyangwa umuntu ku giti cye ashobora kubyikorera wenyine. Hakwiye kuba hariho ubufatanye, gutekerereza hamwe, kubera ko ibiva muri iri koranabuhanga rishya nka AI rigira ingaruka ku Isi yose, ntirigira ingaruka ku kigo cyangwa igihugu kimwe.  Afurika itunze ibirenze kuba isoko rinini Niklas Adalberth, Umuyobozi akaba n uwashinze Norrsken nk Umuryango Mpuzamahanga uhuriza hamwe ba Rwiyemezamirimo bashinze ibigo bitandukanye, yabajije Perezida Kagame impamvu abashoramari bakwiye kubona Afurika nk umugabane wuje ishoramari, amusubiza ko uyu mugabane ufite ibyiza byinshi bingana n iby ahandi ku Isi ndetse bishobora kuba binaruseho. Umukuru w Igihugu yavuze ko abashoramari bakwiye kuzirikana ko Afurika ifite abantu bafite ubwenge n impano nyinshi nk iby abandi bose ku Isi, ziyongeraho n indi mitungo kamere itabarika Ati:  Abashoramari ntibakwiye kureba Afurika nk Isoko rinini gusa nubwo ari ko bimeze, ahubwo ko hari n abaturage bakomeje guharanira iterambere bashobora kuzagera ku biri ahandi hose ku Isi cyangwa bakabirenza. Ikindi abashoramari bakwiye kurebaho ni uko ushora imari ufite intego, kandi iyo ntego iba ikwiye kugerwaho. Harimo inyungu n iterambere uba ushaka kubona, nakwizeza ko ibyo bazabibona.  Perezida Kagame yanahamije ko gushora imari mu Rwanda ari ukwiteganyiriza kuko ari igihugu cyahisemo guharanira kubaka ikirere cy ubucuruzi gitekanye cyoroshya kugera ku ntego yaba iy Abanyarwanda n abandi bose baza gukorana na bo. Yaboneyeho kugaragaza ko urwego Abanyafurika bariho ubwarwo rwisobanurira icyo babura nko kuba bakwigirira icyizere no gukora ibyo bakwiye kuba bakora kugira ngo bagere ku rwego indi migabane igezeho ndetse bakanarurenza. Yanenze Abanyafurika babura gukora ibisabwa bakirukira ku bandi ngo babakemurire ibibazo, ati:  Kwishyira mu murongo wo kwihesha agaciro si ikintu dukwiye kuba dusaba undi uwo ari we wese ngo abidukorere. Ntekereza ko nta muntu n umwe ugufitiye umwenda. Wowe ubwawe wifitiye umwenda. Abanyafurika bifitiye umwenda wo kwizamura maze tugakorana n abandi nk abafatanyabikorwa bari ku rwego rumwe.  Ba rwiyemezamirimo biganjemo urubyiruko, bishimiye amahirwe bagize yo kuganira na Perezida Kagame bakamubaza ibibazo bitandukanye byakomoje no ku buzima bwe bwite. NTAWITONDA JEAN CLAUDE

link204: Minisitiri w Uburinganire n Iterambere ry Umuryango MIGEPROF Dr Uwamariya Valentine, yatangaje ko abakobwa bakwiye kwihatira gukoresha ikoranabuhanga ndetse no kurikoresha mu kwihangira imirimo mu rwego rwo gushyigikira gahunda ya Leta yo kuryimakaza kandi ntawe usigaye inyuma. Yagize ati:  Mbere babwirwaga ko ikoranabuhanga ari iry abahungu, cyangwa ko ari iry abasirimu ariko ubu si ko biri icya mbere ni amakuru, iyo utamenye amakuru kandi na yo aboneka ku ikoranabuhanga ntacyo uba wamenye, ntabwo rero twavuga ngo abakobwa basigare ahubwo nk uko tubishishikariza Abanyarwanda bose turashyiraho umwihariko no ku bakobwa kuko haracyariho imbogamizi . Yongeyeho kandi ko bitavuze ko abahungu bahejwe, ahubwo ari uko abakobwa bagira kwitinya. Ati:  Iyo tuvuga abakobwa ntabwo tuba twibagiwe n abahungu, ahubwo harimo imbogamizi zitandukanye hazamo no kwitinya kw abakobwa kugira ngo tubatinyure, kuko hari n ababikoze bigakunda ntabwo twatera imbere nk igihugu kandi hari igice kimwe cyasigaye . Yagize ati:  Umuryango UN women urimo gushyira imbaraga nyinshi mu gufatanya n abandi bafatanyabikorwa barimo Leta n abikorera kugira ngo dufashe abagore bakiri bato ndetse n abakobwa mu nzego zigifite ibibazo zirimo iz ubukungu, imibereho ndetse no kubigisha uko bakwigirira icyizere bakazavamo abayobozi, muri iki gihe rero turi mu gihe cy ikoranabuhanga no guhanga udushya twakoranye n abafanyabikorwa benshi kugira ngo ibi dutegurira aba bakobwa bizatange umusaruro . Bamwe mu bakobwa bahuguwe bahamya ko aya mahugurwa yatumye batinyuka bahanga imiriro ndetse bahabwa n akazi k ikoranabuhanga bahuguwemo. Vanessa Icyeza yagize ati:  Baduhuguye gukoresha imbuga nkoranyambaga no kubaka imbuga za internet ubu njyewe nabonye akazi nkora imishinga ya internet ndimo gukora umushinga uzafasha ku bitaro mu kumenya amakuru y abarwayi baje kwivuza . Aya mahugurwa ategurwa na UN Women ku bufatanye na Leta y u Rwanda yatangiye guhugura abakobwa n abagore bato kuva mu 2020, ibahugura ku bijyanye no kwihangira imirimo n ikoranabuhanga ryatanga ibisubizo ku bibazo byugarije abaturage aho abagera kuri 400 bahuguwe ndetse bashakirwa n akazi. link205: Minisiteri y Ikoranabuhanga no guhanga Ibishya (MINICT) yatangaje ko bitarenze mu mpera z umwaka wa 2024, serivisi za Leta zirenga 400 ari zo zizaba ziri ku rubuga Irembo rumenyerewe nk amarembo yoroshya imitangire inoze ya serivisi. Byagarutsweho mu gihe hari gahunda yo kongera serivisi 200 kuri urwo rubuga bitarenze muri Kamena 2024, mu gihe nanone MINICT yemeza ko abaturage barenga miliyoni 5 ari bo bakeneye guhugurwa mu birebana no kubyaza umusaruro ikoranabuhanga. Umunyamabanga Uhoraho muri MINICT Iradukunda Yves, yabwiye itangazamakuru ko kugeza ubu serivisi za Leta zitangirwa ku rubuga Irembo zibarirwa hejuru ya 100. Akomeza avuga ko ubumenyi mu ikoranabuhanga ari ingenzi cyane kuko ari bwo buzatuma izo serivisi zishyirwa ku ikoranabuhanga zirushaho gukoreshwa na benshi mu rugendo rwo kwihutisha iterambere. Yagize ati:  Kongera ubumenyi mu ikoranabuhanga ni cyo gishyizwe imbere. Kugira ibikorwa remezo n ibikoresho by ikoranabuhanga ni kimwe, ariko dukeneye n ubushobozi bwo kubikoresha ngo tugere kuri serivisi. Guverinoma y u Rwanda imaze igihe ishyira ku ikoranabuhanga serivisi zinyuranye mu korohereza abaturage kuzigeraho. Yakomeje ashimangira ko intego y amahugurwa atangwa ni ukugira ngo u Rwanda rukomeze kubaka ubukungu bushingiye ku ikoranabuhanga, ati:  Icyo tugamije ni uko serivisi zose za Leta zaba zashyizwe ku ikoranabuhanga bitarenze mu mpera z umwaka  utaha.  Kuri ubu serivisi ziteganyirizwa kongerwa ku rubuga Irembo zirimo gutoranywa mu nzego zitandukanye harimo serivisi z amashyamba, ukwimura amatungo, ibyangombwa byo gufungura ivuriro, ibyangombwa byo gutumiza ibintu mu mahanga, impushya zo gukora ubushakashatsi n izindi zitangwa n Urwego rw Igihugu Ngenzuramikorere (RURA). Mu zindi serivisi zitegurirwa kutangirwa ku Irembo harimo ibyangombwa bimwe na bimwe bitangirwa ku Mudugudu, ku Kagari mo ku rwego rw Umurenge, harimo ibyangombwa by ubugenzuzi, kwishyura serivisi zimwe na zimwe nk iz irimbi, iz isuku, imisanzu y isoko ndetse na serivisi zitangwa n Ikigo NAEB. Iradukunda yavuze ko Leta yahaye ikiranga Ikigo mpuzamahanga IDCL gikora ibijyanye no kunoza ubumenyi mu bakozi, uburezi ndetse no mu baturage. Icyo kigo gitanga impamyabumenyi mu bijyanye no gukoresha mudasobwa mu guharanira ko abakozi ba Leta barushaho kubona ubumenyi buhagije mu bijyanye no gukoresha ikoranabuhanga. Ibyo bibafasha kurushaho kunoza imirimo batanga serivisi zishingiye ku ikoranabuhanga. Ubufatanye bugamije kandi ngo bugamije gukemura ikibazo cy ubumenyi buke mu baturage muri rusange, amahugurwa n impamyabushobozi zitangwa bikaba bishingiye ku byo isoko ry umurimo rikeneye kuri ubu ndetse n amahirwe ahari y iterambere rishya rigenda rivuka. Ni mu gihe kandi u Rwanda rwihaye intego yo kuba rwageze ku baturage barenga 60% bafite ubumenyi mu bijyanye no gukoresha ikoranabuhanga mu guharanira iterambere ryabo rya buri munsi bitarenze mu 2024. Hakomeje gahunda zigamije guhugura abaturage bakabona ubumenyi buhagije mu ikoranabuhanga, by umwihariko mu gukoresha telefoni zigezweho bagera kuri serivisi zitangirwa kuri murandasi, aho urubyiruko rwashyiriweho mu gjtanga ubwo bumenyi ku buntu. Mu bundi bumenyi bwongererwa abaturage habazamo ubujyanye no gukoresha ikoranabuhanga mu buhinzi n ubworozi, mu bucuruzi, mu ishoramari mu buzima n izindi nzego. NTAWITONDA JEAN CLAUDE

Ku wa Kabiri, ni bwo Dr. Kalinda n itsinda ryari rimuherekeje bahuye na Minisitiri w Ububanyi n Amahanga w agateganyo Jalil Abbas Jilani, baganira ku nzego zirimo ubucuruzi, ishoramari no guhererekanya ubunararibonye bushingiye ku muco.
