link241: Mu myaka igera kuri 30 ishize, Ibitaro bya Kabgayi bivura amaso bimaze kwakira no guha serivisi ababarirwa hagati ya miliyoni imwe n igice na miliyoni ebyiri, ugereranyije n abantu bagera kuri 200 byakira buri munsi. Nkurikiyinka Leonard w imyaka 68 y amavuko utuye mu Murenge wa Ruhango, Akarere ka Ruhango, ni umwe muri iyo mbaga y abahawe serivisi zamunyuze, kuri ubu akaba yishimira ko yatandukanye n akaga ko guhuma kari kamwugarije. Mu masaha ashyira saa sita, Nkurikiyinka yicaye ku ntebe hamwe na bagenzi be benshi barimo abazindutse mu museke, buri wese ategereje ko izina rye rigerwaho. Yumvise nomero yatoye akigera ku bitaro mu ndangururamajwi amenya ko ari we ugezweho, ahita yerekeza ku muganga w amaso. Akihagera yasobanuye uburyo inshuro ebyiri amaze kuza kwa muganga zahinduye byinshi kuko ari gusezera ubuhumyi yabonaga bumwugarije, kuri ubu asigaye areba neza nubwo ikibazo asigaranye ari ukutabasha gusoma inyuguti nto. Muganga w amaso yaramusuzumye amwandikira guhabwa indorerwamo z amaso, asohokana icyizere cy uko agiye guca ukubiri no kugira ingorane mu gusoma. Mu kiganiro yagiranye n Imvaho Nshya, Nkurikiyinka yagarutse ku nzira y umusaraba yanyuzemo ubwo yabonaga kurora neza bimuca mu myanya y intoki. Ati:  Nagiraga ikibazo cy uduhwa twazaga mu maso mu gitondo nkarira, nareba umuntu uri imbere yanjye gato simenye uwo ari we. Mu nshuro ebyiri naje kwivuza hari ikintu cyahindutse; nari mfite ibintu by ibihu mu maso byagiye bigabanyuka, umuntu araturuka hariya nkamumenya. Ikibazo nari nsigaranye ni icyo kutareba mu bitabo neza, na bwo bankoreye ibizamini banyandikira indorerwamo z amaso.  Nkurikiyinka ashimira abaganga b Ibitaro bya Kabgayi bivura amaso ubunyamwuga bagaragaza bita ku barwayi, agashishikariza abantu bose kujya bihutira kwa muganga mu gihe bumvise mu jisho hari ikibazo kuko abaganga bemeza ko nta nsimburajisho iraboneka. Ati:  Ni ukuri abaganga bita ku barwayi b amaso ndabashimira kuko batanga serivisi nziza, n ukihagera bwa mbere rwose ntibamurindagiza barakuyobora bakakurangira aho ujya kwaka imiti. Abafite ubwoba ko kubaga bibabaza nabamara impungenge ko bagutera ikinya mu jisho, ntumenya uko byagenze. Abantu benshi bagira ubwoba ngo kubaga birababaza, nta kintu bibabazaho rwose bagomba kuza kwa muganga bakisuzumisha iyo basanze ari ngombwa barabavura.  Mutumyinka Jacqueline utuye mu Murenge wa Byimana mu Karere ka Ruhango, na we yishimira ko inshuro ya mbere yageze ku Bitaro bya Kabgayi bivura amaso yahaboneye serivisi nziza bituma atahana icyizere cyo gukira vuba. Yagize ati:  Numvaga ndwaye amaso, andya, hakaba ubwo ntabasha kureba nkumva n umutwe urandya nyine mpitamo kuza kwivuza; usibye ko nabyumvaga gusa ni bwo bwa mbere nari nje ntabwo nari mbizi ko ndwaye.  Akomeza avuga ko ubuhumyi ari ikintu gikomeye cyane, kuko butuma umuntu yibagirwa Isi yari azi agasigara ayishushanya mu mutwe we gusa. Ati:  Se ubwo iyo utareba uragira ngo ibindi byose ntibiba bipfuye? Ntabwo wabasha kwigira mu kazi bisanzwe, ntacyo wabasha gukora nyine, iyo utarora uba ukeneye umuntu ukurandata  Dr. Livin Uwemeye, Umuganga w inzobere mu Bitaro bya Kabgayi bivura amaso, yavuze ko nubwo umubare munini w Abanyarwanda bumva neza agaciro k ubuvuzi bw amaso, hari benshi baza kwa muganga bakererewe kandi ijisho riri mu bice by umubiri bitihangana igihe kinini. Yavuze ko uko umuntu akererwa bituma n amahirwe yo kongera kubona neza agenda agabanyuka, ati:  Nkaba nsaba rero ababyeyi ndetse n abantu bakuru muri rusange, ko igihe umuntu agize ikibazo agomba kwihutira kugana ubuvuzi bw amaso bumwegereye kuva ku kigo nderabuzima kugera ku bitaro. Ijisho ni urugingo rutoya ariko rutihangana, iyo rero umuntu agize ikibazo agashyiramo ibyatsi cyangwa akigurira imiti, ashobora kwangiza byinshi kurusha uko byari bimeze.  Yahishuye ko uretse indwara z amaso zishobora gutuma umuntu ahuma, hari n izishobora gutuma atakaza ubuzima igihe yaba ativurije igihe, harimo nka kanseri y amaso n izindi ndwara zigaragarira mu maso ariko zifite ibindi bice by umubiri zafashe, ndetse n impanuka za hato na hato. Amateka na serivisi zitangirwa mu Bitaro bya Kabgayi bivura amaso Ibitaro bya Kabgayi bivura amaso ni ishami ry Ibitaro Bikuru bya Kabgayi ryatangiye mu mwaka wa 1993, rishinzwe na Diyosezi ya Kabgayi ku bufatanye n Umuryango wa Gikirisitu CBM. Byatangiye bifite inshingano yo gufasha no kuvura abaturage benshi mu Rwanda bari bafite ikibazo cy amaso ariko batabonaga uko bivuza. Dr. Theophile Tuyisabe, inzobere mu buvuzi bw amaso akaba n Umuyobozi w Ibitaro bya Kabgayi bivura amaso, avuga ko yari serivisi nshyashya kandi ikenewe cyane mu Bitaro bya Kabgayi biri ku rwego rw Akarere. Iyo serivisi yavuye ku rwego rw Akarere igera ku rwego rw Igihugu bita urwa gatatu (Referral Hospital) guhera mu mwaka wa 2012. Nubwo ari ishami ry Ibitaro bya Kabgayi, rifite urwego rwihariye (centre sp cialis ) mu buvuzi bw amaso, ari na yo mpamvu rifite uburenganzira n ubushobozi bwo kwakira abarwayi baturutse mu Turere twose tw Igihugu boherejwe ngo babone serivisi zisumbuyeho. Dr. Tuyisabe yavuze ko batanga serivisi zitandukanye zirimo gusuzuma amaso bisanzwe, aho umuntu wese urwaye ndetse n ushaka kwisuzumisha bitabwaho uko bikwiye. Gusuzuma ni serivisi yiyongeraho gutanga indorerwamo z amaso (Lunettes) zihabwa umuntu wese bigaragaye ko ari ngombwa kuzihabwa, yaba akiri muto cyangwa ari mukuru. Dr. Tuyisabe ati:  Hanyuma kuri ibyo hiyongeraho serivisi zo kubaga amaso. Iyo serivisi yo kubaga amaso ni umwihariko wa Kabgayi kuko turagerageza tugashaka abaganga b inzobere kandi bameze neza ku rwego rw Igihugu, ku buryo baba batanga serivisi zifatika. Ni yo mpamvu uyu munsi ushobora kuza ugasanga hagati y abantu 20 na 30 barabazwe ku munsi wagereranya n abantu nka 150 baza kwisuzumisha kuri uwo munsi ugasanga ko ari umubare ufatika kandi ukeneye koko abantu b inzobere babishoboye.  Indi serivisi y umwihariko ku Bitaro bya Kabgayi mu buvuzi bw amaso mu Rwanda ni iyitwa  low vision  cyangwa  basse vision  igarurira umuntu ubushobozi bwo kubona neza mu gihe ubundi buvuzi bwose butakunze. Dr. Tuyisabe yakomeje agira ati:  Hari udukoresho dufite dushobora kongerera inyuguti ubunini. Wa muntu wabonaga gakeya, akaba ashobora gusoma nka Bibiliya, ubutumwa buje muri telefoni n ibindi.  Hakurikiraho urwego rw ibizamini bikorerwa amaso akeneye ibipimo birenze ibisanzwe. Ibitaro bya Kabgayi bifite imashini zo ku rwego rwo hejuru zipima ijisho mu buryo bwimbitse, hamenyekana serivisi ya nyayo ijisho ryari ryananiranye rikwiriye guhabwa. Ikindi kintu cyihariye ku Bitaro bya Kabgayi bivura amaso ni uko umuntu mukuru yivuriza ukwe n abana bakivuriza ukwabo. Ibyo ngo byakorewe kurushaho kunoza serivisi zihabwa buri wese mu cyiciro cye, by umwihariko abana bakabona amahirwe yo kuvurwa bishimiye gukina no kuganira na bagenzi babo ari na ko barindwa kuba bakwandurira izindi ndwara mu kavuyo k abantu benshi.
link242: Kuva taliki 25 kugeza ku ya 26 Kanama 2022, Ihuriro rya 5 ku bufatanye n itangazamakuru ry u Bushinwa n Afurika ryabereye i Beijing mu Bushinwa mu buryo bwa interineti (Iyakure) . Iri huriro ryari rifite insanganyamatsiko igira iti  Icyerekezo gishya, Iterambere rishya n Ubufatanye bushya.  Iri huriro ryateguwe n ubuyobozi bukuru bwa Radiyo na Televiziyo by u Bushinwa, Guverinoma y abaturage ya Beijing hamwe n Umuryango Nyafurika w itangazamakuru. Intumwa zirenga 240 zaturutse mu nzego zitandukanye za Leta, mu bigo by itangazamakuru rishinzwe gutunganya amajwi n amashusho, Abadiporomate intumwa zabo baturutse mu Bushinwa n abagize Komisiyo y umuryango w ubumwe bw Afurika yita ku Itangazamakuru igizwe n ibihugu 42 bitabiriye ihuriro. Perezida w u Bushinwa, Xi Jinping na Perezida wa Senegal, Macky Sall ari nawe uyoboye Umuryango w Ibihugu by Afurika Yunze Ubumwe ubu (African Union ) bohereje ubutumwa bw ishimwe muri iri huriro, aho baganiriye cyane ku ruhare rwiza rw iryo huriro mu guteza imbere ibiganiro n ubufatanye hagati y itangazamakuru ry u Bushinwa n Itangazamakuru ry  Afurika, guteza imbere imyigire hagati y imico no gushimangira ingamba nyazo z ubufatanye hagati y Ubushinwa na Afurika. Ubu butumwa bwo kongera imbaraga nshya mu bufatanye bw itangazamakuru ry u Bushinwa n iry Afurika mu bihe biri imbere. Inama yari yitabiriwe kandi na Iradukunda Yves, Umunyamabanga Uhoraho muri Minisiteri y ikoranabuhanga no guhanga udushya, wari watumiwe muri iri huriro, yavuze ko yishimiye kuryitabira. Mu myaka icumi ishize, u Rwanda, kimwe n ibindi bihugu by  Afurika, rwungukiye byinshi muri ubu bufatanye bw itangazamakuru ry u Bushinwa n irya Afurika, harimo ishoramari n ibikorwa remezo, kugeza TV hose, kubaka ubushobozi, guhanga imirimo n ibibndi byinshi bigezweho. Ku bijyanye no guteza imbere itumanaho hagati y u Rwanda n u Bushinwa yagize ati:  U Rwanda rwashyizwe ku mwanya wa 2 muri Afurika mu rwego rwo koroshya ishoramari muri raporo ya Banki y Isi ishinzwe ubucuruzi muri 2020 kuba ku mugabane w  Afurika, ubukungu bushingiye ku bikorera mu Rwanda bwatanze isura nziza ku bashaka gushora imari zabo ku mugabane kubera ko inzitizi zo kwinjira zisa nkaho zitagihari. Turizera ko tuzabona sosiyete z Abashinwa zishora imari mu bikorwa remezo, nk inganda za TV , imishinga y ubucuruzi igezweho. Kugira ngo hagabanyuke igiciro cyo kugeza ibintu muri Afurika kikiri hejuru, kandi hakorwe ubushakashatsi ku iterambere kugira ngo haboneke ibisubizo bikwiye ku masoko nyafurika  n ahandi.  Uyu mwaka hijihijwe isabukuru y imyaka 10 y ihuriro ry ubufatanye bw itangazamakuru ry u Bushinwa n iry Afurika. Mu gushimira byimazeyo no gusubiza amaso inyuma ku musaruro w ibisubizo byiza, ku mpande zombi bagezeho mu myaka icumi ishize, Inzego za Leta impande zombi zashyizeho uburyo bunoze bw itumanaho kugira ngo bahurize hamwe politiki n ibitekerezo bya buri wese. Imiryango n amashyirahamwe y itangazamakuru bakoze ubufatanye mu gutangaza amakuru ndetse no mu bindi bikorwa bitandukanye birimo umushinga wo kugeza TV za Satelite mu midugudu 10,000 hamwe n undi mushinga wa  Integrated Digital Switch-over Project  byihutishije iterambere mu rwego rw itumanaho muri Afrika, ibintu byagiriye cyane Afurika akamaro kanini. U Bushinwa bwatanze kandi gahunda zitandukanye z amahugurwa y inzobere mu bitangazamakuru byo muri Afurika busangiza ubumenyi bufatika no gushimangira ihanahana ry abakozi. Ubufatanye hagati y impande zombi buragenda burushaho kwagura amashami ku muvuduko wo hejuru, mu bice bitandukanye. Ubufatanye mu bitangazamakuru ku mpande zombi bashyigikiye, guteza imbere indangagaciro rusange z abantu no gushyiraho gahunda y ibitekerezo by iterambere mu bufatanye mpuzamahanga. Itangazamakuru ry u Bushinwa n Afurika kandi rizateza imbere guhuza udushya no kurushaho kunoza ubufatanye mu bijyanye n ikoranabuhanga rya digitale n ubukungu mu ikoranabuhanga hagamijwe gushimangira kungurana ibitekerezo, gusangira amahirwe no kuzamura ubushobozi bw imiyoborere. Muri iyi nama yamaze iminsi ibiri gusa, hamuritswemo bimwe mu bikorwa byagezweho muri iyi myaka 10 ishize y Ubufatanye bw itangazamakuru ry u Bushinwa n iry Afurika (2012-2022).  Ihuriro ryasohoye itangazo rikubiyemo icyerekezo na gahunda bigamije iterambere ry itangazamakuru mu gihe kizaza, hashyirwaho n ingamba 5 zirimo guteza imbere ubufatanye n itumanaho, gushyigikira iterambere ry Isi, gutangaza inkuru z ubufatanye hagati y u Bushinwa n Afurika, guteza imbere itangazamakuru ry ikoranabuhanga no gushimangira ihanahana ry amakuru mu rubyiruko.

link244: Umuryango w Abanyarwanda baba muri Congo-Brazzaville n inshuti z u Rwanda, ku wa Mbere taliki ya 4 Nyakanga 2022 bahuriye mu birori bibereye ijisho byo kwizihiza isabukuru ya 28 yo Kwibohora,bashimira Ingabo za RPA Inkotanyi zakuye Igihugu mu icuraburindi ryatewe n ubuyobozi bubi. Ni ibirori byitabiriwe n abasaga 300 biganjemo Abanyarwanda batuye mu Mujyi wa Brazzaville, inshuti zabo, abagize inzego zitandukanye z ubuyobozi, abahagarariye ibihugu byabo n Imiryango mpuzamahanga muri Congo. Ambasaderi w u Rwanda muri Repubulika ya Congo Th oneste Mutsindashyaka, yashimiye abitabiriye uwo muhango by umwihariko inshuti z u Rwanda zifatanyije na bo kwishimira iterambere ryagezweho mu Gihugu no mu bubanyi n amahanga mu myaka 28 ishize. Yavuze ko ukwibohora nyako k u Rwanda gushoboka gusa habayeho ubufatanye n ubutwererane biboneye mu ruhando mpuzamahanga. Yagize ati:  Ni yo mpamvu  u Rwanda rwizera cyane ko ubufatanye bw ibihugu bikiri mu nzira y amajyambere, butanga umusaruro ku mpande zose, ari ingenzi mu kugera ku iterambere u Rwanda n ibihugu by abavandimwe by Afurika bikeneye.  Yavuze ko Ingabo zahoze ari iza RPA Inkotanyi zamaze imyaka ine ziyagoheka, amajoro azira ibitotsi, abatabarika batakaje ubuzima muri urwo rugendo rwo kubohora u Rwanda, byarangiye bageze ku ntsinzi bahagaritse Jenoside yakorerwaga Abatutsi yahitanye abasaga miliyoni mu minsi 100 y ukwezi kwa Mata kugeza muri Nyakanga 1994. Yagize ati:  Uyu munsi duha icyubahiro abantu bose bagize uruhare muri urwo rugamba rwo kubohora Igihugu cyacu. Intekerezo zacu nanone zihora ku batanze igitambo kiruta ibindi cy ubuzima kugira ngo tube tugeze hano turi. Iya 4 Nyakanga mu 1994, ni bwo igice cyijimye kurusha ibindi mu mateka yacu cyasoje, hatangira kubakwa amateka mashya aho Abanyarwanda bahindutse umwe, aho buri wese abaho kandi agakorera mu mutekano n umutuzo, yishimira kuba afite uburenganzira busesuye. Yavuze ko amateka mabi u Rwanda rwanyuzemo ari yo arusunikira gutanga umusanzu wo kubungabunga amahoro mu bihugu by Afurika no hanze y uyu mugabane kugira ngo hatazagira ahandi ku Isi ayo mateka yakongera kwisubira. Yavuze kandi ko muri iyi myaka 28 ishize, u Rwanda rwahindutse kimwe mu bihugu bifite umuvuduko uhambaye mu iterambere ry ubukungu, icyitegererezo mu kwimakaza uburinganire n iterambere ry umugore, ubuyobozi butagira n umwe buheza, ikoranabuhanga no kubungabunga ibidukikije. Yakomeje agira ati:  Mbese, uyu munsi ni uw ibyishimo, umunezero w iterambere ridasanzwe ryagezweho mu myaka 28 ishize. Ni ishema kandi ku Banyarwanda bose babaye muri iryo terambere umunsi ku wundi. Ariko u Rwanda ruzirikana ko ukwibohora nyako kubaho gusa mu bufatanye mpuzamahanga.  Yashimangiye ko ari yo mpamvu u Rwanda na Congo Brazzaville bikomeje kwimakaza umubano mwiza biyobowe n Abakuru b Ibihugu byombi Perezida Paul Kagame na mugenzi we Denis Sassou Nguesso. Yanakomoje ku ruzinduko Perezida Kagame aheruka kugirira i Brazzaville n ahitwa Oyo mu kwezi kwa Mata uyu mwaka, rushimangira uburyo ibihugu byombi bikomeje guharanira ko umubano bifitanye warushaho kubyazwa umusaruro mu nyungu z ibihugu byombi. Muri urwo ruzinduko, hasinywe amasezerano y ubufatanye mu nzego zitandukanye z iterambere, harimo ubutwererane mu bya Politiki, ubukungu, ubuhinzi, guhanahana umuco n ubuhahirane bw abaturage, kubungabunga ibidukikije, ubufatanye mu bucukuzi no kubungabunga umutungo kamere n ibindi. Abitabiriye ibirori basusurikijwe n itsinda ry ababyinnyi ry Inganzo Ngali ryaturutse mu Rwanda. Umugoroba wose wari wuzuye amajwi y ingoma, indirimbo n imbyino gakondo, Abanyarwanda bongera kwihuza n umurage ndetse n umuco gakondo ubaranga aho bari hose ku Isi.
link245: Amazi ni umusingi ukomeye mu buzima bwa muntu kandi kuyakoresha neza biri mu by ibanze mu kugera ku iterambere rirambye. Mu Rwanda, hari intambwe igaragara imaze guterwa mu kurushaho kunoza uburyo abaturage bagerwaho n amazi binyuze mu kurinda umutungo kamere w amazi, gukumira icyakwanduza amazi, no gukumira imyuzure. Intambwe imaze guterwa mu kugeza amazi ku baturage no kuyakwirakwiza yagezweho binyuze muri Gahunda ikomatanyije yo gucunga umutungo kamere w amazi yagize uruhare rukomeye cyane mu kugera kuri Politiki y u Rwanda yo kubaka ubukungu butangiza ibindukikije no guhangana n Imihindagurikire y Ikirere, uburyo bukurikira uko ari butandatu zigaragaza uko u Rwanda rucungamo amazi mu guhangana n imihindagurikire y ikirere. 1. Gushinga ikigo gishinzwe Umutungo Kamere w Amazi mu Rwanda (RWB) Ikigo gishinzwe Umutungo Kamere w Amazi mu Rwanda (RWB) cyashyizweho mu mwaka wa 2020 hagamijwe guharanira ko haboneka amazi ahagije kandi abungabunzwe neza mu guharanira iterambere rirambye. Iki kigo gishinzwe gushyira mu bikorwa politiki z Igihugu, amategeko na gahunda birebana n umutungo kamere w amazi, kugenzura igenamigambi rihuriweho ry umutungo w amazi, gufata amazi no kurwanya isuri, gutanga impushya zo gucunga amazi, guhangana n imyuzure no guteza imbere ububiko bwayo. Iki kigo kandi kigenzura kandi imikoreshereze n imicungire myiza y amazi. Ishyirwaho ry Ikigo gishinzwe Umutungo Kamere w Amazi mu Rwanda rigaragaza ubushake bwa Guverinoma bwo kubungabunga amazi n akamaro kayo mu guhindura imibereho n ubukungu by Igihugu. Byinshi ku birebana n Ikigo gishinzwe Umutungo Kamere w  Amazi mu Rwanda wabisanga kuri www.rwb.rw. 2. Ishyirwaho ry impushya mu gukoresha umutungo kamere w amazi Gukenera gukoresha Umutungo kamere w amazi mu Rwanda bikomeje kwiyongera kandi Igihugu gikeneye kumenya ingano y amazi akoreshwa, abayakoresha, uburyo bayakoreshamo ndetse n aho bayakoresha. Iyo ibyo bimaze kumenyekana, bishobora kugereranywa n ingano y amazi ihari ndetse n ikwiye gukoreshwa hagamijwe gucunga uyu mutungo kamera neza kandi mu buryo burambye. Itegeko rigenga imikoreshereze n imicungire y umutungo kamere w amazi mu Rwanda riha Ikigo cy Igihugu gishinzwe Umutungo Kamere w  Amazi mu Rwanda (RWB) ububasha bwo gukusanya amakuru yose akenewe mu kunoza imicungire y amasoko y amazi. Imitangire y impushya ku mikoreshereze y uwo mutungo kamere ni bumwe muri ubwo bubasha cyahawe. Kubera iki hatangwa impushya mu gukoresha umutungo kamere w amazi?   Gucunga neza umutungo kamere w amazi:  Gucunga neza ikoreshwa ry umutungo kamere w amazi no kwimakaza ibikorwa bitanga inyungu mu guteza imbere ubukungu bw Igihugu.   Gusaranganya umutungo kamere w amazi mu buryo bungana: Mu rwego rwo gusaranganya kugira ngo babashe kugabura amazi, abashinzwe umutungo kamere w amazi bagomba kumenya ingano y amazi aboneka, n uburyo asanzwe akoreshwa.   Kubungabunga ibidukikije: Abashinzwe umutungo kamere w amazi bagomba kumenya neza ko amazi akoreshwa neza, mu buryo buteguye neza, kandi ko ibiyanduza byagabanyijwe ku buryo bufatika. Mu gihe cyo gutanga umutungo kamere w amazi kugira ngo ukoreshwe mu buryo butandukanye, abashinzwe uwo mutungo bagomba guharanira ko uruhererekane rw ibidukikije rukomeza kuboneka. Imitangire y ibyangombwa ikorwa hifashishijwe ikoranabunga (application) rifasha abakoresha amazi gusaba ibyangombwa bakeneye. Iyo mikorere ya serivisi zo gutanga ibyangombwa ifasha mu micungire iboneye y umutungo kamere w amazi. Ibyo byangombwa ushobora kubigeraho unyuze kuri www.waterpermit.rwb.rw. 3. Gahunda yo gufata no kubika amazi U Rwanda rufite imvura nyinshi ku kigero cya mm 1,200 buri mwaka, bituma gufata amazi y imvura buba ubundi buryo bwo kubona amazi mu rwego rwo guhaza ubusabe bw amazi bukomeza kwiyongera, guharanira iterambere ry imibereho n ubukungu ndetse no kubungabunga ibidukikije. Nubwo bimeze bityo ariko, u Rwanda rukomeza gufatwa nka kimwe mu bihugu bifite amazi make bitewe n ubushobozi buke bwarwo bwo kuyabika. Imishinga itari mike yashyizwe mu bikorwa kugira ngo iyi ntego igerweho kandi yose yagaragaje ko hari amahirwe menshi yo gufata amazi y imvura mu gihugu hose. Nk uko bigaragara muri raporo nshya mu gufata no kubika amazi, mu Rwanda haboneka uburyo butatu bw ingenzi butari karemano bwo kubika amazi. Muri bwo harimo ibyuzi by amazi bikoreshwa mu kuhira imyaka ku buso buto, ibibumbiro, ibidamu n ingomero zifashishwa mu kubyara ingufu z amashanyarazi. Iyi Raporo yagaragaje ko kuri ubu u Rwanda rufite ibyuzi by amazi 1,414 bifite ubushobozi bwo kubika metero kibe 131,603, ibyanya by ingomero 77 bifite ubushobozi bwo kubika metero kibe miliyoni 8 n ibidamu 50 bifite ubushobozi bwo kubika metero kibe miliyoni 75. Hakomeje gushyirwa imbaraga mu kongera ubushobozi bw Igihugu bwo  kubika amazi, no kunoza uburyo bwo gufata amazi mu ngo z abaturage. 4. Ubufatanye mu gucunga umutungo kamere w amazi Kwimakaza imicungire y umutungo kamere w amazi mu igenamigambi ry Uturere Hagati y umwaka wa 2017 na 2018, GGGI   umuryango mpuzamahanga ufasha ibihugu biri mu nzira y iterambere kugera ku bukungu burambye harangerwa ibidukikije, yafashije Uturere mu gutegura gahunda z iterambere ryatwo tuzagenderaho kugeza mu mwaka wa 2024. GGGI yatanze inzobere kugira ngo zitange ubujyanama bwimbitse mu itegurwa rya za gahunda z iterambere mu mijyi 6 yunganira Umujyi wa Kigali ari yo Huye, Muhanga, Musanze, Nyagatare, Rubavu na Rusizi. GGGI yaharaniye ko mu igenamigambi ry Uturere mu iterambere hitabwa by umwihariko ku micungire iboneye y umutungo kamere w amazi binyuze muri gahunda ikomatanyije yo kubungabunga umutungo w amazi (IWRM) ifatwa nk ikora ku nzego zose zigira uruhare mu iterambere rirambye ry Akarere. Ibikorwa byihariye birimo kwita kurinda inkengero z imigezi, kongera umubare w ingo zifite ibigega n ubundi buryo bwo gufata amazi y imvura n ibindi. Ibyo biteganyijwe kuba ingirakamaro mu rugendo rwo kugeza amazi meza ku baturage, kuhira imyaka mu buryo bugezweho, gukora ubuhinzi bugamije ubucuruzi, no gutanga amahirwe y inyongera yo kugera ku iterambere rirambye. Umushinga w amazi mu iterambere ry u Rwanda   Water for Growth Rwanda  Umushinga w imyaka ine  Water for Growth Rwanda  (W4GR) watangiye mu mwaka wa 2017, uri mu bufatanye bw ibihugu by u Rwanda n u  Buholandi, ukaba warafashije Minisiteri y Ibidukikije gushyira mu bikorwa gahunda ikomatanyije yo kunoza imicungire n imikoreshereze y umutungo kamere w amazi. Intego nyamukuru yari iyo kugeza umutungo kamere w amazi kuri bose, mu buryo bunoze kandi bubungabunga ibidukikije ku buryo burambye. Umushinga W4GR wakoze gahunda zo gufata amazi kuri 30% by ubuso bw igihugu, zirimo n igenamigambi rirambuye ryo gukwirakwiza amazi mu bihe bitandukanye kugeza mu mwaka wa 2050. Kuri ubu u Rwanda ruzi ingano y amazi ishobora gukoreshwa mu kuhira imyaka, mu nganda, mu bworozi, mu mirimo yo mu ngo ndetse no ku bidukikije. Ayo makuru yavuye mu bushakashatsi yahishuye ikibazo cy amazi make inerekana ko hakenewe ivugururwa mu gishushanyombonera cya gahunda yo kuhira ndetse no muri Politiki igenga umusaruro w ibiribwa. Uyu mushinga kandi wanafashije gushyiraho Ikigo gishinzwe Umutungo Kamere w Amazi mu Rwanda (RWB), ari na cyo kigenzura ikwirakwizwa ry amazi mu kwirinda amakimbirane, kunoza ubuziranenge bw amazi, kuvugurura ibyanya bifata amazi, gukumira no kurwanya isuri, gushyiraho ingamba zo guhangana n imyuzure mu gihe cy imvura ndetse n amapfa mu gihe cy izuba. Umushiga Ukomatanyije w Imicungire y Umutungo Kamere w Amazi- IUCN Intego y Umushinga Ukomatanyije w Imicungire y Umutungo Kamere w Amazi (IWRM) ni iyo gushyira mu bikorwa imicungire irambye y amazi n ibishanga no kwinjiza urusobe rw ibinyabuzima muri gahunda ya IWRM hagamijwe gushyigikira kugabanya ubukene, iterambere rigera kuri bose, guhangana n imihindagurikire y ikirere no kubungabunga ibinyabuzima bitandukanye. Uyu mushinga ufite inzego esheshatu uzibandaho ari zo:   Kunoza imiyoborere n imicungire y ibikorwa by amazi   Gushora imari mu bikorwa remezo by umutungo kamere w amazi   Kwimakaza uruhare rw amazi mu iterambere   Kongera ubumenyi ku mutungo kamere w amazi mu Rwanda   Kwimakaza Imikoranire myiza n ubufatanye mu gukoresha no gucunga neza umutungo kamere w amazi   Imihindagurikire y Ikirere, uburinganire, abantu n uburenganzira 5. Kunoza gahunda zo kurwanya no kwirinda imyuzure mu mijyi Mu guhangana n ibibazo by imyuzure mu Mujyi wa Kigali n indi mijyi mu gihugu, hatangijwe gahunda zitandukanye. Ikigo gishinzwe Umutungo Kamere w Amazi mu Rwanda (RWB) cyubatse Sitasiyo 15 zitanga amakuru yizewe ku nkengero z amazi mu bihe bitandukanye. Ibyo bifasha mu gukurikirana za ruhurura n ahandi hantu hibasirwa n imyuzure bigatuma hafatwa ingamba hakiri kare. Hubatswe ruhurura zisaga 40, hakorwa ubugenzuzi ngo hamenyekane ingo zituye aho zishobora kwibasirwa n umwuzure bituma imiryango isaga 5,000 yari ituye mu manegeka yashobora gushyira ubuzima bwabo mu kaga yimurirwa mu bice bitekanye. 6. Kubungabunga no kuvugurura ibishanga Kwangirika kw ibishanga ndetse no kwandura kwabyo byagize ingaruka zikomeye ku buziranenge bw amazi n ingano yayo. Igabanyuka ry ubushobozi bw ibishanga bwo gusigasira urusobe rw ibinyabuzima rutandukanye ritera ubwiyongere bw imyuzure rigatwara n ubuzima bw abantu, ibikorwa remezo bikangirika, umusaruro w ubuhinzi ukagabanyuka ndetse n amazi agakama. Ni yo mpamvu u Rwanda rwimakaje gahunda yo kuvugurura ibishanga, by umwihariko mu bice by imijyi. U Rwanda rwageze kuri byinshi bikurikira mu micungire y ibishanga, birimo:   Ivugururwa ry ibikorwa by ingenzi bigize uruhurirane rw ibishanga. Nk urugero, ivugururwa ry igishanga cy Urugezi guhera mu mwaka wa 2005 ryatumye cyongerwa ku rutonde rw ibishanga bigengwa n amasezerano ya RAMSAR ku Isi, ndetse kinabona igihembo mpuzamahanga mu 2010.   Imishinga minini yo kongera gusana ibishanga irimo icyiciro cya kabiri cy Umushinga wo Guteza Imbere Imijyi (RUDPII), Uwo gushyira mu byiciro ibishanga byose no kwimura inganda zabarizwaga mu cyanya cyahariwe inganda cyari mu gishanga zerekezwa Masoro mu kindi cyanya aho zibereye kuba.   Himuwe kandi ibikorwa by ubucuruzi bisaga 6,000 (amagaraji y imodoka, parikingi n inganda) n ibikorwa by ingo bikurwa mu bishanga byari mu mujyi kugira ngo byongere gutunganywa.   Itegurwa ry igishushanyombonera cy ibishanga ryerekanye ko nibura kilometero kare 15, zigize 20% by ibishanga byo mu mijyi bizongera gusanwa, mu gihe 29% byamaze kwemezwa nk ibigomba gukoreshwa mu buryo burambye, 38% bigafasha mu kubungabunga urusobe rw ibinyabuzima hanyuma ahasigaye hakifashwa mu bukerarugendo no kuruhuka. Ikindi kintu cy ingenzi cyagezweho ni icyo gutunganya igishanga cya Nyandungu mu Mujiyi wa Kigali, mu buryo bufasha guhangana n imihindagurikire y ikirere kandi bubereye ubukerarugendo, cyashyizwe mu bikorwa n Ikigo cy Igihugu gishinzwe Kubungabunga Ibidukikije (REMA) nyuma y ishoramari ryakozwe n Ikigega cy Ibidukikije mu Rwanda    FONERWA (Rwanda Green Fund), Ishami ry Umuryango w Abibumbye ryita ku Bidukikije (UN Environment) na Leta y u Butaliyani. Iki cyanya cya Nyandungu kiri kuri hegitari 120 kikaba kirimo ibikorwa bitandukanye nk ibyuzi bikozwe mu buryo bw umutako, amashyamba atewe mu buryo bubereye ijisho, ubusitani burimo ibihingwa byifashishwa mu buvuzi, uduhanda tw abanyamaguru dushashe neza ndetse n inzira z amagare, resitora, ishakiro ry amakuru ndetse n ahagenewe izindi serivisi zijyanye no kuruhuka. Uyu mushinga ntiwateguriwe gutanga inyungu z ubusabane n ubukungu gusa, ahubwo unashyigikira uburyo bushya bwo gusubiranya no kubungabunga urusobe rw ibinyabuzima rubarizwa mu bishanga, bikajyana no kwimakaza imicungire irambye y umutungo kamere.
link246: Amashyamba yo mu Rwanda abarirwa ku buso bwa hegitari 724,695 zingana na 30.4% by ubuso bwose bw Igihugu nk uko bitangazwa muri raporo ya vuba igaragaza ubutaka buriho amashyamba (Rwanda Forest Cover Mapping Report/2019). Muri ayo mashyamba 53% ni ayatewe, 21 ni aya cyimeza ari mu mukenke, 19% ni amashyamba ya cyimeza yo mu misozi ibonekamo imvura nyinshi   mu gihe 6.2% ari ibihuru. Kongera ubuso buteyeho amashyamba biri mu bikorwa n imishinga by u Rwanda bigamije kongera ubushobozi bwo guhangana n imihindagurikire y ikirere, kubyaza ubukerarugendo amadovize menshi, kongera umusaruro ukomoka ku bimera no kuzamura imibereho y Abanyarwanda muri rusange. Buri mwaka Abanyarwanda batera amamiliyoni y ibiti muri gahunda ngarukamwaka bafite intego imwe yo kubungabunga amashyamba no kongera umusaruro. Gahunda y Igihugu y Ubukungu Butangiza Ibidukikije yatangijwe mu mwaka wa 2011 nk uburyo burambye buyobora Igihugu ku kubaka iterambere rizira guhumanya ikirere bitarenze mu mwaka wa 2050. Ni gahunda yimakaza agaciro k amashyamba kandi ikubiyemo ingamba 14 zirimo no gutera ibiti no kubungabunga amashyamba mu buryo burambye hagamijwe guharanira ko amashyamba ya Leta n ay abantu ku giti cyabo acungwa mu buryo bwiza kandi burambye. Bimwe mu byagezweho muri Gahunda y Igihugu y Ubukungu Butangiza Ibidukikije, by umwihariko mu mushinga urambye wo gutera ibiti no kubungabunga amashyamba ni ibi bikurikira: 1. Ubuso buriho amashyamba mu Rwanda bwageze kuri 30.4% Binyuze mu cyerekezo cy Igihugu na politiki yo kureba kure heza, u Rwanda rwabaye kimwe mu bihugu byatangiye hakiri kare gushyira mu bikorwa Intego y Isi yose yiswe  Bonn Challenge  yo kugarura amashyamba ku butaka yahozeho kugeza kuri hegitari zisaga miliyoni 150 bitarenze mu mwaka wa 2020, na hegitari miliyoni 350 bitarenze mu 2030. Mu mwaka wa 2011, ni bwo u Rwanda rwihaye intego yo kugarura amashyamba kuri hegitari miliyoni ebyiri yahozeho akaba yarangijwe bitarenze mu 2020. Imbaraga u Rwanda rwashyize mu kubungabunga amashyamba ariho, gutera amashyamba mashya, kuvugurura amashyamba mu bice bitandukanye by Igihugu no guharanira kugera ku ntego za Bonn Challenge ni byo byatumye u Rwanda rugera ku ntego yo kugira 30.4% by ubuso bw Igihugu buriho amashyamba. Izo nzego zifite akamaro gakomeye ko gushimangira uruhare rw u Rwanda mu guhangana n imihindagurikire y ikirere. Kuri ubu hashyizwe ingufu mu gutera ibiti ahahurira abantu benshi mu mijyi itandukanye y u Rwanda nk uko bigaragara mu gishushanyombonera kirimo gukoreshwa ubu aho Icyerekezo 2050 gitegeka ko imijyi yose n amasanteri agenda atera imbere bikwiye kuba ifite ibyanya byahariwe amashyamba bifatanye n ubundi butaka bukorerwamo ibikorwa bitandukanye. Igihugu nanone cyashyizeho ahatunganyirizwa Ingemwe z Ibiti (Tree Seed Centres) muri pepiniyeri ziherereye mu Karere ka Gatsibo n Aka Huye, mu rwego rwo kongera ingemwe z ibiti zuzuje ubuziranenge. Aha hatunganyirizwa ingemwe z ibiti hagira uruhare mu micungire y amashyamba, umusaruro  w amakara yo gucana, ibiti byifashishwa mu bwubatsi, gukoresha izindi ngufu zitangiza ibidukikije no kubona ingemwe zujuje ubuziranenge by umwihariko. Ni ihuriro kandi ry ibikorwa bigize uruhererekane rwo gutunganya no gukwirakwiza ingemwe, birimo gukora ubwoko bushya, kunoza ubwoko busanzwe, kubungabunga utunyangingo tw ibiti, gukusanya ingemwe, kuzirera no kuzikwirakwiza. Nanone kandi zizakomeza kubakira ku ntsinzi yo kuvugurura amashyamba y u Rwanda no gushyigikira imbaraga zashyizwe mu buhinzi bw amashyamba mu bice bitandukanye mu Gihugu. 2. Gahunda ngarukamwaka yo gutera ibiti n Umuganda Leta y u Rwanda yashoye akayabo mu gutera amashyamba mashya no kuyasubiza aho yari asanzwe binyuze muri gahunda ngarukamwaka yo gutera ibiti n amashyamba. Nko mu gihembwe cy umwaka wa 2020/2021 Abanyarwanda bateye ibiti miliyoni 25 byagize uruhare mu kuvugurura amashyamba muri gahunda yo guhangana n imihindagurikire y ikirere. Muri icyo gihembwe, hegitari 7,400 zateweho ibiti bisanzwe, izindi hegitari 900 zihingwaho ibiti mu mashyamba ya cyimeza ndetse haterwa n ibiti byeraho imbuto 77,000. Hanavuguruwe hegitari 500 z amashyamba ahingwamo ibiti bicanwamo amakara mu rwego rwo kongera umusaruro. Biteganyijwe ko muri uyu mwaka hazaterwa ibiti bibarirwa muri miliyoni 43. Igikorwa ngarukakwezi cy Umuganda na cyo gihuriza hamwe abaturage mu Nzego z ibanze bagamije kugera ku musaruro uhuriweho. Umuganda ni gahunda yihariye y Igihugu yahaye abaturage amahirwe yo kugira uruhare mu gutera ibiti mu rwego rwo kongera ubuso bw Igihugu buteweho amashyamba no kubungabunga ibidukikije uhereye mu Nzego z ibanze. Hagati y umwaka wa 2009 n uwa 2019, ubuso buriho amashyamba bwiyongereyeho 27.7% byose bikaba umusaruro wa gahunda zitandukanye zo gutera amashyamba mashya no kuvugurura ayari yarangijwe. 3. Kwegurira (gukodesha) abikorera amashyamba yari aya Leta mu kuyacunga neza Binyuze muri gahunda y Igihugu yo kwegurira abikorera ibikorwa bimwe, Leta y u Rwanda yagiranye ubufatanye n urwego rw abikorera mu guharanira imicungire iboneye y amashyamba ya Leta. Minisiteri y Ibidukikije yatangije ubufatanye bwayo bwa mbere n abikorera bujyanye no gucunga amashyamba mu mwaka wa 2019, kuyabungabunga no kongera umusaruro atanga. Kugeza ubu Hegitari 23,456.15 zingana na 38.4% by amashyamba ya Leta zicungwa n abashoramari bigenga binyuze mu masezerano y igihe kirekire basinyanye na Leta. 4. Ihangwa rya Pariki y Igihugu ya Gishwati-Mukura U Rwanda ruherutse guhanga Pariki y Igihugu ya Gishwati-Mukura, imwe muri Pariki nshya muri Afurika, mu rwego rwo kurinda amashyamba kimeza ya kera n inguge ziyacumbitsemo.Iyo Pariki igizwe n amashyamba abiri ari yo irinini rya Mukura n irito rya Gishwati aherereye ku musozi ugabaya icyogogo cy imigezi ya Congo na  Nili, agakurikira urwunge rw ibibaya by Albertine (Albertine Rift) bigizwe n urusobe rw ibinyabuzima rutandukanye. Kuvugurura ishyamba rya Gishwati-Mukura no kurihindura Pariki byashobotse ku bufatanye na Global Environment Facility/GE na Banki y Isi, binyuze mu Mushinga wa LAFREC (Landscape Approach to Forest Restoration and Conservation) washyizwe mu bikorwa n Ikigo cy Igihugu cyo kubungabunga Ibidukikije (REMA), Urwego rushinzwe Iterambere mu Rwanda (RDB) n Uturere iyo Pariki iherereyemo. Uwo mushinga w imyaka 5 wubakiye ku mirimo yakozwe na  Forest of Hope Association , ugera ku ntego yo kuvugurura Gishwati-Mukura binyuze mu kuhindura ahantu nyaburanga mu rwego rwo kurushaho kubungabunga urusobe rw ibinyabuzima ruhabarizwa no kwegereza imiryango ituriye Pariki inyungu urwo rusobe rutanga. Kuri ubu RDB irimo gutegura gahunda iri mu byiciro bitandukanye ijyanye no kubungabunga urwo rusobe rw ibinyabuzima no guteza imbere ubukerarugendo muri Pariki y Igihugu ya Gishwati   Mukura. Iyo gahunda ikubiyemo kuyiha abayirinda, gukaza ingamba zo kuyibungabunga, guteza imbere ubushakashatsi, ubufatanye na Koperative ziyakoreramo, gukemura amakimbirane y abantu n inyamaswa, kugenzura imiterere y ibidukikije no guteza imbere ubukerarugendo bugendera ku mategeko. Iyi gahunda irimo gutegurwa ku bufatanye n Inzego z ibanze ndetse n Ikigo  Imizi , Ishami rya   Wilderness Safaris. 5. Kwagura Pariki y Igihugu y Ibirunga U Rwanda rwatangiye umushinga ukomeye wo kwagura Pariki y Igihugu y Ibirunga no guharanira ahazaza heza h ingagi zo mu misozi zita mu rugo ishyamba ry Ibirunga. Iyi gahunda y imbonekarimwe igamije kwagura pariki ku kigero cya 23% ikiyongeraho kilometero kare 37.4, ubunini bwayo bukava kuri kilometero kare 160 bukagera kuri kilometero kare 197.4. Biteganyijwe ko izo hegitari zizongerwaho izindi hegitari 6,620 z icyanya cy ubuhumekero (buffer zone) gitandukanya Pariki n ubutaka bw abaturage. Pariki y Igihugu y Ibirunga ifite urusobe rw ibinyabuzima rudatekanye kandi buri kuri kilometero kare 160 gusa, ari na yo mpamvu u Rwanda rwiyemeje kuyagura ikongerwaho hafi kimwe cya kane cy ubunini ifite ubu. Pariki yagutse yitezweho guteza imbere imibereho y ingagi zo mu misozi zitagiraga ubwisanzure buhagije kandi ishyigikire ubwiyongere bwazo ku kigero kiri hagati ya 15% na 20% n igabanyuka ry imfu z abana b ingagi ku kigero kiri hejuru ya 50%. Kwagura Pariki y Igihugu y Ibirunga byitezweho no guhindura imibereho y imiryago iyizengurutse kandi bizanatuma gusura ingagi birushaho kuba ubunararibonye buhebuje. Byinshi ku bijyanye no kwagura Pariki y Igihugu y Ibirunga wabisanga kuriwww.visitrwanda.com/gorillas.

Akomeza agira ati:  Leta ishora amafaranga menshi mu bikorwa remezo bijyanye no korohereza abantu kugira internet yihuta, kuko Leta yifuza ko imbuga nkoranyambaga zibyazwa umusaruro mu buryo bwiza, hirindwa kuzikoresha ibyaha kuko amategeko ahana ibyo byaha ahari.  RIB isaba abakoresha imbuga nkoranyambanga kuzikoresha neza birinda kwinjira mu buzima bwite bw abantu, gukoresha imvugo zikurura inzangano, gutukana, gutangaza amakuru y ibihuha ndetse no gukwirakwiza amashusho y urukozasoni. Umuvugizi wa RIB agira ati:  Ntabwo kugira urubuga nkoranyambaga umuntu yigengaho bitanga ubudahangarwa bwo kuba azakurikiranwa mu gihe azikoresheje nabi.
link264: Akenshi iyo umuntu yitabye Imana ibye biba birangiye,imishinga ye igahagarara, ariko Abanyarwanda bavuga ko nta muhanzi upfa bitewe n uko ibihangano bye bikomeza kumvwa bikananyura benshi. Iryo iserukiramuco rizabera muri BK Arena tariki 26 Ukwakira 2024, rikazatangira guhera saa munani z amanywa, aho ibikorwa byose bizasozwa n igitaramo kizatangira saa moya z ijoro, hakazanamurikirwamo indirimbo Yvan Bravan yasize zitarasohoka. link265: Umuhanzi w indirimbo zo kuramya no guhimbaza Imana, Israel Mbonyi yaciye agahigo ko kuba umuhanzi nyarwanda wa mbere ukurikirwa n abantu benshi ku rubuga rwa Youtube. link266: Umukinnyi wa filime uri mu bakunda kugarukwaho cyane ku mbuga nkoranyambaga, Inkindi Aisha uzwi cyane nka Aisha, avuga ko impamvu abakobwa basigaye bikundira abasaza kurusha uko bakunda abasore bari mu kigero kimwe ari uko babitaho cyane nk abana bibyariye. Ati:  Umukobwa ari mu mihango urugero, nta kunyitaho nta n imbuto urimo kumushyira, nta kotekisi igura igihumbi wanzaniye, ariko urimo kumubarira iminsi ngo uzamuhamagare aze kugusura! link267: Umusizi akaba n umunyamuziki Igihozo Sylvie avuga ko yifuza kumenyekana nk umuhanzi n umusizi icyarimwe nta gisize ikindi kuko ari wo mwihariko we. Akenshi usanga umuntu iyo afite impano zirenze imwe, agira iyo akunda kurusha izindi, ku buryo ari nayo ahitamo kwimenyekanishamo, bitandukanye cyane n uko Igihozo Sylvie abitekereza kuko yumva yabikora byombi. Akomeza agira ati:  Sinakubwira ko hari icyo nshaka kumenyekanamo kurusha ikindi kuko umuziki ndawukunda kandi ndawukora, ibisigo nabyo ni uko, byombi nifuza kubimenyekanaho kuko ari wo mwihariko wanjye. Ati :  Imvune zo zirimo, ariko Umunyarwanda yaravuze ngo utayihinganye ntayishira, umwanzuro wanjye ni uko ntagomba kurambirwa, niba uyu munsi bitameze neza, ntabwo ngomba gucika intege, uko igisigo kije nkandika, n indirimbo yaza nkandika, kuko ni bwo nzagera ku cyo nshaka.  Uyu muhanzi akaba n umusizi avuga ko abakobwa n abagore badakwiye gucika intege kuko gukora biherekejwe no gusenga byose bigerwaho. Igihozo azwi mu ndirimbo zitandukanye zirimo Umunyarwandakazi, Nyamibwa, Ramba Rwanda ndetse n iyo aherutse gushyira ahagaragara yitwa Urukundo. Uretse izo ndirimbo uyu muhanzi akaba n umusizi anafite ibisigo birimo Urukundo, Nazize iki, Urugero n ibindi.

link270: Mu Rwanda hagiye kubera inama izahugurirwamo abahanzi ku bijyanye n uko bakora umuziki ucuruza ndetse ukarenga urwego rw Igihugu ukagera ku ruhando mpuzamahanga bitewe n ubufatanye hagati y abahanzi. Access music in Africa ni inama yateguwe na Music in Africa binyuze muri Minisiteri y Urubyiruko n Iterambere ry Ubuhanzi, ikazahuza abahanzi b Abanyarwanda n abandi bazaba baturutse mu bihugu bitandukanye byo ku mugabane w Afurika. Mu kiganiro n itangazamakuru cyabaye tariki 11 Ukwakira 2024, abanyamakuru bagaragarijwe ko ari amahirwe ku bahanzi nyarwanda nkuko Uncle Austin uri mu bahanzi bazitabira iyi nama abisobanura. Yagize ati:  Maze imyaka irenga 20 ndi mu ruganda rw imyidagaduro, ariko ndashimira Minisiteri y Urubyiruko n Iterambere ry Ubuhanzi kubera amahirwe yo kugaragaza impano batanga. Mu bihe byacu iyo tugira amahirwe nk aya umuziki wacu ubu uba ugeze kure. Umuyobozi mukuru wa Music in Africa ari nayo itegura iyo nama, Eddie Hatitye avuga ko bahisemo gukorera iyi nama mu Rwanda kubera ko ari Igihugu kirimo kuzamura umuziki wacyo, kandi gifite abahanzi bazi akazi kabo. Asaba abahanzi ko bakwiye kumenya ko umuziki atari ibintu biraho bidafite akamaro, ko ahubwo umuziki ari akazi gatanga amafaraga nk ubundi bucuruzi, kandi ko biteguye gufasha abahanzi nyarwanda kubisobanukirwa. Umunyamabanga wa Leta muri Minisiteri y Urubyiruko n Iterambere ry Ubuhanzi Sandrine Umutoni, asaba abahanzi kwiyandikisha bakazitabira iyi nama, kuko bazayungukiramo byinshi. Ati:  Ni amahirwe menshi cyane ku bahanzi bacu, ni ukuvuga ngo ubu turimo kubamenyesha ko bitakiri ngombwa ko umenyekana hanze y u Rwanda kuko wagiye gushaka ayo mahirwe oya, ayo mahirwe yabizaniye, icyo basabwe ni ukwiyandikisha ku rubuga rwabugenewe.  Yongeraho ati:  Niba uri umuhanzi ngwino witabire ibyo biganiro, umenye icyo usabwa kugira ngo ugere ku rwego rwisumbuyeho, kandi abazayitabira bagomba kumva ko bazaba baje guhatana bakagaragaza ko mu Rwanda naho hari impano kandi ishobora gukundwa, kuko hazaba hari n abandi bahanzi b ahandi, guhatana ni ngombwa ukerekana ko ushoboye.  Iyi nama izamara iminsi itatu, uhereye tariki 14-16 Ugushyingo 2024, ikazabera muri Convetion Center na Mundi Center, ikazaba ihuje abahanzi 20 bavuye mu bihugu bisaga 15 by Afurika, ikazanaherekezwa n ibitaramo. Mu bahanzi bo mu Rwanda bamaze kwiyandikisha harimo Uncle Austin, Ariel Wayz, Busahari, Ish Kevin n abandi. Inama ya Access Music in Africa imaze kubera mu bihugu bitandukanye birimo Kenya, Ghana, Afurika y Epfo n ahandi akaba ari bwo bwa mbere  igiye kubera mu Rwanda.
